nei o ratou, nga turi he taringa nei o ratou.

<span id="an_43:9">43:9</span> Kia huihui nga iwi katoa, kia rupeke tahi
nga tauiwi: ko wai i roto i a ratou hei whakaatu i tenei, hei korero i
nga mea o mua ki a tatou? kia homai e ratou o ratou kaiwhakaatu, kia
whakatikaia atu ai ta ratou: ma ratou ranei e whakarongo, e mea mai, He
pono.

<span id="an_43:10">43:10</span> Ko koutou hei whakaatu mo taku, e ai ta
Ihowa, me taku pononga i whiriwhiria e ahau, kia mohio ai koutou, kia
whakapono ai ki taku, kia matau ai ko ahau ia, kahore he Atua i
whakaahuatia i mua i ahau, kahore hoki tetahi i muri i ahau.

<span id="an_43:11">43:11</span> Ko ahau, ko ahau nei ano, a Ihowa;
kahore atu hoki he kaiwhakaora, ko ahau anake.

<span id="an_43:12">43:12</span> Naku i whakaatu, naku hoki i whakaora,
naku ano i korero, i te mea kahore he atua ke i roto i a koutou: na ko
koutou hei kaiwhakaatu moku, e ai ta Ihowa, a ko te Atua ahau.

<span id="an_43:13">43:13</span> Ae ra, i te mea kahore ano he ra ko
ahau tenei; e kore hoki tetahi e whakaora ake i roto i toku ringa: maku
e mahi, ko wai hoki hei whakakahore?

<span id="an_43:14">43:14</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a to koutou
kaihoko, a te Mea Tapu o Iharaira, He whakaaro ki a koutou i unga
tangata ai ahau ki Papurona, a ka mauria mai e ahau ratou katoa, he
mawhiti mai, ara nga Karari i runga i nga kaipuke i harakoa ai ratou.

<span id="an_43:15">43:15</span> Ko Ihowa ahau, ko to koutou Mea Tapu,
ko te kaihanga o Iharaira, ko to koutou Kingi.

<span id="an_43:16">43:16</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa nana nei i
homai te ara i te moana, te huarahi i roto i nga wai kaha;

<span id="an_43:17">43:17</span> Nana nei i whakaputa mai te hariata, te
hoiho, te ope, me te kaha; takoto tahi ana ratou, te ara ki runga: kua
keto ratou, kua tineia, ano he muka.

<span id="an_43:18">43:18</span> Kaua e mahara ki nga mea o mua; ko nga
mea onamata kaua e whakaaroa.

<span id="an_43:19">43:19</span> Tenei ahau te mahi nei i te mea hou;
akuanei te tupu ai: e kore ranei e mohiotia e koutou? ka oti i ahau he
ara i te koraha, he awa i te titohea.

<span id="an_43:20">43:20</span> Ka whakakororiatia ahau e nga kararehe
o te parae, e nga kirehe mohoao, e nga otereti; no te mea ka hoatu e
ahau he wai i te koraha, he awa i te titohea, hei inu ma taku iwi, ma
taku i whiriwhiri ai;

<span id="an_43:21">43:21</span> Ma te iwi i whakaahuatia e ahau maku,
ma ratou e kauwhau te whakamoemiti moku.

<span id="an_43:22">43:22</span> ¶ Na kihai nei koe i karanga ki ahau, e
Hakopa; kua hoha koe ki ahau e Iharaira.

<span id="an_43:23">43:23</span> Kihai i kawea mai e koe ki ahau au hipi
hei tahunga tinana; kihai ano ahau i whakakororiatia ki au patunga tapu.
Kahore aku whakamahi i a koe ki te whakahere, kihai ano koe i ngenge, i
te meatanga i te whakakakara.

<span id="an_43:24">43:24</span> Kihai i hokona e koe he kakaho reka
maku ki te moni, kihai hoki ahau i makona i te ngako o au patunga tapu;
engari i whakamahia ahau e koe ki ou hara, mauiui ana ahau i au mahi he.

<span id="an_43:25">43:25</span> Ko ahau, ko ahau nei ano, te kaimuru
atu i ou he, he whakaaro ano ki ahau: e kore ano ou hara e maharatia e
ahau.

<span id="an_43:26">43:26</span> Whakamaharatia ahau; tatou ka whakawa
ki a tatou ano; korerotia e koe tau, kia whakatikaia ai koe.

<span id="an_43:27">43:27</span> Ko tou papa tuatahi, i hara; ko ou
kaiwhakaako, whakakeke ana ki ahau.

<span id="an_43:28">43:28</span> Na reira whakapokea iho e ahau nga
rangatira o te wahi tapu, a hoatu ana e ahau a Hakopa ki te kanga, a
Iharaira ki te tawai.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> ¶ Na whakarongo, e taku pononga, e
Hakopa, e Iharaira, e taku i whiriwhiri ai.

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a tou kaihanga,
nana nei koe i whakaahua i roto i te kopu, mana nei koe e awhina, Kaua e
wehi, e Hakopa, e taku pononga, e Iehuruna, e taku i whiriwhiri ai.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> No te mea ka ringihia e ahau he wai ki
runga ki te tangata matewai, he awa ki te wahi maroke: ka ringihia e
ahau toku wairua ki ou uri, taku manaaki ki tau whanau.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> A ka tupu ratou i waenga taru, ano he
wirou i te taha o nga rerenga wai.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Ka ki ake tenei, Na Ihowa ahau; ko tetahi
atu, karangatia ana e ia ko Hakopa hei ingoa mona; ko tetahi atu,
tuhituhi ana tona ringa ki a Ihowa, whakahuatia ake e ia ko Iharaira hei
ingoa mona.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a te Kingi o
Iharaira, a tona kaihoko ano, a Ihowa o nga mano, Ko ahau te tuatahi ko
ahau ano te mutunga; Kahore atu hoki he atua, ko ahau anake.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Ko wai hoki hei rite moku, hei karanga,
hei whakaatu, hei whakarite kia noho rarangi, mai o toku whakaritenga i
te iwi onamata? a ma ratou e whakaatu nga mea meake puta mai, me nga mea
ano e puta a mua.

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> Kaua e wehi, kaua e pawera: kihai ianei i
korerotia e ahau ki a koe nga mea onamata, i whakaaturia hoki? ko koutou
ano hei kaiwhakaatu moku. Tera atu ranei tetahi atua ke? ae ra, kahore
he kamaka; kahore ahau e mohio ki tetahi.

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> ¶ Ko nga kaiwhakaahua o te whakapakoko,
he horihori katoa ratou; kahore hoki he pai o a ratou mea ahuareka: ko o
ratou kaiwhakaatu kahore e kite, kahore e mohio; e whakama ai ratou.

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Ko wai te kaiwhakaahua o tetahi atua,
te kaiwhakarewa ranei o te whakapakoko kahore nei ona pai?

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Nana, ko ona hoa katoa, ka whakama: ko
nga kaimahi ano, he tangata nei ratou: kia huihui mai ratou katoa, tu
ai. Ka wehi, ka whakama ngatahi.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> E hangaia ana e te parakimete he toki,
ka mahi i roto i nga waro, whakaahuatia ana e ia ki te hama, puta ana te
kaha o tona ringa ki te mahi i taua mea; ka hemo ano ia i te kai, kore
noa iho he kaha; kahore e inu i te wai, mauiui noa iho.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> Ko te kamura, whakamarokia mai ana e ia
te aho, tuhia iho e ia ki te pene, mahia ana e ia ki te waru; tohungia
ana e ia ki te kapehu, mahia ana e ia kia rite ki te ahua o te tangata,
ki te ataahua ano o te tangata; hei mea mo roto i te whare.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> Tuaina ana e ia he hita mana, tikina
ana e ia te kaiperi, me te oki, a whakapakaritia ana e ia mana tetahi i
roto i nga rakau o te ngahere; whakatokia ana e ia te ahe hei whakatupu
ma te ua.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> Katahi ka waiho hei wahie ma te
tangata: ka tangohia hoki e ia tetahi wahi hei whakamahana i a ia; ina,
whakaungia ana e ia, hei tunu taro; na kei te hanga ano ia i tetahi
atua, koropikoria atu ana e ia; mahia ana e ia hei whakapakoko, tapapa
to nu atu ki reira.

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> Ko tetahi wahi o taua rakau, e tahuna
ana e ia ki te ahi, ko tetahi wahi, hei mea i te kikokiko hei kai mana;
tunua ana e ia tana e tunu ai, a ka makona: ae ra, ka mahana ano ia, a
ka mea, Ha, kua mahana ahau, kua kite i te ahi.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Ko te toenga, hanga ake e ia hei atua,
hei whakapakoko mana: tapapa ana ia, koropiko ana, inoi ana ki taua mea,
ka mea, Whakaorangia ahau; ko koe nei hoki toku atua.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> Kahore ratou e mohio, kahore e mahara;
no te mea kua araia e ia o ratou kanohi kei kite, o ratou ngakau kei
matau.

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> Kahore hoki e anga ake te ngakau o
tetahi, kahore e mohio, kahore e matau, e ki ake ai ia, Ko tetahi wahi o
tenei i tahunga e ahau ki te ahi; i tunua ano e ahau he taro ki ona
ngarahu, tunua ana e ahau he kikokiko, kainga ake e ahau; a kia meing a
e ahau te toenga o taua rakau hei mea whakarihariha? me tapapa ranei
ahau ki te take rakau?

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Ko tana kai, he pungarehu; kua
tinihangatia tona ngakau, a ngau ke ana ia, te whakaora ia i tona
wairua, te ki ake ranei, Kahore ranei he korero teka i toku matau?

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> ¶ Kia mahara ki enei, e Hakopa, e
Iharaira; he pononga hoki koe naku; naku koe i whai ahua ai, he pononga
hoki koe naku: e Iharaira, e kore koe e wareware i ahau.

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> Ko ou he, murua ake e ahau, me te mea
he kapua matotoru; ko ou hara, me te mea he kapua: hoki mai ki ahau;
naku hoki koe i hoko.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> Waiata, e nga rangi, he mahi hoki tenei
na Ihowa. Hamama, e nga wahi o raro rawa o te whenua. Kia pakaru mai ta
koutou waiata, e nga maunga, e te ngahere, e nga rakau katoa o reira; no
te mea kua oti a Hakopa te hoko e Ihowa, kua whai kororia ia i a
Iharaira.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a tou
kaihoko, nana nei koe i whai ahua ai, no roto mai ano i te kopu, Ko
Ihowa ahau, ko te kaihanga o nga mea katoa, naku anake nga rangi i hora,
naku i takoto ai te whenua: ko wai toku hoa?

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> Ko nga tohu a te hunga korero teka he
ana i a ia, ko nga tohunga tuaahu whakahaurangitia ana e ia; ko te hunga
whakaaro nui, whakahokia ana e ia ki muri, ko to ratou matauranga,
whakapoauautia iho.

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> Mana pu i a ia te kupu a tana pononga,
te whakaaro a ana karere rite rawa i a ia; ko tana kupu ki Hiruharama,
Ka nohoia koe; ki nga pa o Hura, Ka hanga koutou; maku ano e whakaara
ona wahi kua ururuatia.

<span id="an_44:27">44:27</span> Ko tana kupu ki te rire, Kia mimiti:
maku ano e whakamaroke ou awa.

<span id="an_44:28">44:28</span> Ko tana kupu mo Hairuha, He hepara ia
naku, ka rite ano i a ia taku katoa i pai ai; mana hoki e ki ki
Hiruharama, Ka hanga koe; a ki te temepara, Ka whakatakotoria ou
turanga.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa ki tana i
whakawahi ai, ki a Hairuha, he mea pupuri nei naku tona ringa matau, kia
pehia ai e ia nga iwi ki raro i a ia; maku ano e wewete to nga hope o
nga kingi; ko nga tatau ka whakapuaretia ki tona aroaro; e kore ano nga
kuwaha e tutakina.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Ko ahau e haere i mua i a koe, ki te
whakatikatika i nga wahi tapokopoko: ko nga tatau parahi ka pakaru i
ahau; ka tapahia ano e ahau nga tutaki rino.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Ka hoatu ano e ahau ki a koe nga taonga o
te pouri, me nga mea huna o nga wahi ngaro, kia mohio ai koe ko Ihowa
ahau, e whakahua atu nei i tou ingoa, ko te Atua o Iharaira.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> He whakaaro naku ki taku pononga, ki a
Hakopa, ki a Iharaira, ki taku i whiriwhiri ai, na reira koe, tou ingoa,
i karangatia ai e ahau: whakahuatia ana e ahau tou ingoa i te mea kahore
ano koe kia mohio ki ahau.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> ¶ Ko Ihowa ahau, kahore atu hoki; kahore
ke atu he atua, ko ahau anake: maku koe e whitiki, ahakoa kahore koe i
mohio ki ahau:

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> Kia mohio ai te hunga i te rawhiti, me o
te uru, kahore atu, ko ahau anake. Ko Ihowa ahau, kahore ke atu.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> Naku te marama i whai ahua ai, naku i
hanga te pouri; ko ahau te kaihohou rongo, te kaihanga ano o te kino: ko
ahau, ko Ihowa, te kaimahi o enei mea katoa.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> Maturuturu iho, e nga rangi i runga; kia
ringihia mai ano he tika e nga kapua; kia puare te whenua, kia hua te
whakaora, kia wana ngatahi te tika; naku, na Ihowa, taua mea i hanga.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Aue te mate mo te tangata e totohe ana ki
tona Kaiwhakaahua! He maramara rihi i roto i nga maramara rihi o te
oneone! E mea ake ranei te paru ki tona kaiwhakaahua, He aha tau e mahi
na? e mea ranei tau i hanga ai, Kahore ona ringa?

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> Aue te mate mo te tangata e mea ana ki
tona papa, He aha tau kua whanau nei? ki te wahine ranei, He aha te mea
ka whakamamae na koe?

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a te Mea
Tapu o Iharaira, a tona Kaiwhakaahua ano, Uia mai ki ahau nga mea e puta
mai a mua; ko nga meatanga ki aku tamariki, ki te mahi hoki a oku ringa,
whakahaua mai ahau e koe.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> Naku i mahi te whenua, i hanga hoki nga
tangata o runga: naku, na oku ringa i hora nga rangi; ko o ratou mano
katoa he mea whakahau naku.

<span id="an_45:13">45:13</span> Naku ia i whakaara ake i runga i te
tika, maku ano e whakatikatika ona ara katoa: ko ia hei hanga i toku pa,
hei tuku i aku parau kia haere, kahore hoki he utu, kahore he moni
whakapati, e ai ta Ihowa o nga mano.

<span id="an_45:14">45:14</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Ko nga mauiui
o Ihipa, ko nga taonga hokohoko o Etiopia, ko nga Tapeani, he tangata
roroa, ka tae mai ki a koe, a ka riro i a koe; ka whai ratou i a koe; ka
tae mekameka mai, ka piko ki a koe, ka mea, He pono kei roto i a koe te
Atua, kahore atu hoki, kahore he Atua.

<span id="an_45:15">45:15</span> He pono he Atua koe e whakangaro ana i
a koe, e te Atua o Iharaira, e te Kaiwhakaora.

<span id="an_45:16">45:16</span> Ka whakama, ae ra, ka numinumi kau
ratou katoa; ka riro ngatahi ki te whakama nga kaimahi o nga
whakapakoko.

<span id="an_45:17">45:17</span> Ko Iharaira ia, ka ora i roto i a
Ihowa, he whakaoranga pumau tonu. E kore koutou e whakama, e kore e
numinumi a ake ake.

<span id="an_45:18">45:18</span> Ko te kupu hoki tenei a Ihowa, a te
kaihanga o nga rangi; ko ia te Atua; nana i whakawhaiahua te whenua,
nana i mahi; nana i whakapumau, kihai i hanga e ia hei takoto kau, i
whakaahuatia e ia hei nohoanga. Ko Ihowa ahau, kahore ke atu.

<span id="an_45:19">45:19</span> Kihai ahau i korero i te wahi ngaro, i
te wahi pouri o te whenua; kihai ahau i mea ki te uri o Hakopa, Rapua
ahau, he mea noa iho. Ko taku korero, ko ta Ihowa, kei te tika, e
whakaatu ana i nga mea e rite ana.

<span id="an_45:20">45:20</span> ¶ Huihui, haere mai, whakatata ngatahi
mai, e nga oranga o nga iwi: kahore he mohio o te hunga e mau ana i te
rakau o ta ratou whakapakoko, e inoi ana ki te atua e kore nei e
whakaora.

<span id="an_45:21">45:21</span> Whakaaturia, kawea mai kia tata, kia
whakatakoto whakaaro ngatahi ratou: na wai tenei i korero i mua riro na
wai i whakaatu i nga wa onamata? He teka ianei naku, na Ihowa? Kore atu
hoki he atua, ko ahau anake; he Atua tika, he kaiwhakaora; kahor e ke
atu, ko ahau anake.

<span id="an_45:22">45:22</span> Tahuri mai ki ahau, kia ora ai koutou,
e nga pito katoa o te whenua: ko te Atua hoki ahau, kahore ke atu.

<span id="an_45:23">45:23</span> Kua waiho ahau e ahau ano hei oati; kua
puta atu te kupu i toku mangai i runga i te tika, e kore ano e hoki mai,
ara ka tuturi nga turi katoa ki ahau, ka oati mai ano nga arero katoa;

<span id="an_45:24">45:24</span> Ka mea mai tetahi ki ahau, Kei a Ihowa
anake te tika, te kaha: ka haere mai ki a ia nga tangata, a ko nga
tangata katoa i riri ki a ia ka whakama.

<span id="an_45:25">45:25</span> Ma Ihowa ka tika ai, ka whakamanamana
ai te uri katoa o Iharaira.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> ¶ Kua piko a Pere, kua tuohu a Nepo; kei
runga i te kirehe, i te kararehe a ratou whakapakoko: ko nga mea e haria
haeretia ana e koutou ka meinga hei kawenga, hei taimaha ki te kararehe
mauiui ra.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> Tuohu ana ratou, piko ngatahi ana; kihai
i taea te pikaunga te pupuri, heoi ko ratou nei ano ka riro hei parau.

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Whakarongo ki ahau, e te whare o Hakopa,
e nga morehu katoa o te whare o Iharaira, he mea waha nei koutou naku no
te kopu mai ano, he mea pikau no roto mai ra ano i te puku.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> Tae noa atu ki to koutou koroheketanga ko
ahau tenei, ka pikaua ano koutou e ahau a hina noa; naku i mahi, maku
ano e mau, maku ano e pikau, maku ano e whakaora.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> ¶ Ki ta koutou kei to wai he ahua moku?
ko wai e rite ana ki ahau? me whakarite ahau ki a wai, e kotahi ai to
maua ahua?

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> Ko te hunga e tahoro ana i te koura i te
peke, e pauna ana i te hiriwa ki te pauna, kei te utu i te kaitahu
koura, hanga ake e ia hei atua; tapapa ana ratou, koropiko ana.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> Amohia ana ia e ratou i runga i te
pokohiwi, pikaua ana, kua waiho e ratou ki tona wahi, tu ana ia; te taea
e ia te nekeneke atu i tona wahi: ka karanga ano hoki tetahi ki a ia,
heoi e kore ia e whakahoki kupu, e kore e whakaora i a ia i roto i t ona
mate.

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> Mahara ki tenei, whakatane, whakahokia ki
te ngakau, e te hunga poka ke.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> Maharatia nga mea tuatahi onamata: ko
ahau hoki te Atua, kahore ke atu; ko ahau te Atua, kahore hoki tetahi
hei rite moku.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> I te timatanga e whakaatu ana i nga mea
o te mutunga, a i nga wa onamata ko nga mea kahore ano i meatia; i ki
ahau, Ko te whakaaro i whakatakotoria e ahau mau tonu, ka oti ano i ahau
taku katoa i pai ai.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> Ka karangatia hoki e ahau he manu kai
kino i te rawhiti, ko te tangata kei a ia toku whakaaro i te whenua
tawhiti; ina, kua korerotia nei e ahau, ka whakaputaina ano e ahau; kua
takoto i ahau, ka oti ano i ahau.

<span id="an_46:12">46:12</span> Whakarongo ki ahau, e te hunga ngakau
pakari, e matara atu ana i te tika:

<span id="an_46:13">46:13</span> Ka kawea mai e ahau toku tika kia tata;
e kore e matara atu; e kore ano taku whakaora e roa; ka whakawhiwhia ano
e ahau a Hiona ki te whakaora, mo Iharaira, mo toku kororia.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> ¶ Haere iho, e noho ki te puehu, e te
tamahine wahine a Papurona: e noho ki te whenua, kahore he torona, e te
tamahine a nga Karari; e kore hoki koe e kiia i muri he kiri angiangi,
he whakatarapi.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> E mau ki nga kohatu mira, hurihia he
paraoa: tangohia ake tou arai, huhua ake te waewae, kia takoto kau te
huha; e whiti i nga awa.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Ka kitea ou wahi e takoto tahanga ana, ae
ra ka kitea tou mea e whakama ai koe: ka rapu utu ahau, e kore ano e
whakaae ki tetahi tangata.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> Ko to tatou kaihoko, ko Ihowa o nga mano
tona ingoa, ko te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> Noho kupukore, haere ki te pouri, e te
tamahine a nga Karari; e kore hoki koe e kiia i muri, ko te wahine
rangatira o nga kingitanga.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> I riri ahau ki taku iwi, i whakapokea
toku kainga tupu; tukua ana e ahau ki tou ringa; kihai i puta tou aroha
ki a ratou, whakataimahatia rawatia iho e koe tau ioka ki te kaumatua.

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> ¶ I mea ano koe, Hei wahine rangatira
ahau ake ake: na kihai noa iho tou ngakau i mea ki enei mea; kihai koe i
mahara ki tona mutunga.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> Na whakarongo aianei ki tenei, e te
wahine e whai na ki nga ahuareka, e noho kore wehi na, e mea na i roto i
tou ngakau, Tenei ahau, kahore atu hoki, ko ahau anake; e kore ahau e
noho pouaru, e kore ahau e mohio ki te matenga o nga tamariki.

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> Otira ka pa whakarere enei e rua ki a koe
i te ra kotahi, te matenga o nga tamariki, te pouarutanga; ka pa enei ki
a koe i tona tonuitanga, ahakoa te nui o au mahi makutu, te maha rawa o
au whaiwhaia.

<span id="an_47:10">47:10</span> I whakawhirinaki hoki koe ki tou kino,
i mea, Kahore he kaititiro moku: ko ou whakaaro nui me tou mohio, na ena
koe i whakangau ke; i mea ai koe i tou ngakau, Ko ahau tenei, kahore ke
atu, ko ahau anake.

<span id="an_47:11">47:11</span> Mo reira ka tae mai te kino ki a koe, e
kore tona putanga e mohiotia e koe, ka taka ano te he ki a koe, e kore e
taea e koe te karo; ka tae hohoro mai ano ki a koe te whakangaro, e kore
e mohiotia e koe.

<span id="an_47:12">47:12</span> Tena ra, e tu, me au whaiwhaia, me au
makutu maha, i mahia ra e koe i tou tamarikitanga ake, me kahore koe e
whai pai, me kahore tau e taea.

<span id="an_47:13">47:13</span> Kua hoha koe i te maha o nga whakaaro i
whakatakotoria e koe. Tena ra, kia tu nga kaiwhakaaro ki nga rangi, nga
kaititiro ki nga whetu, nga mea mohio ki nga marama, kia whakaorangia
koe e ratou i nga mea meake tupono ki a koe.

<span id="an_47:14">47:14</span> Nana, ka rite ratou ki te kakau witi,
ka wera i te ahi; e kore ratou e ora i te ngaunga a te ahi: ehara i te
ngarahu hei whakamahanatanga, ehara hoki i te ahi hei painatanga.

<span id="an_47:15">47:15</span> Na ka pera nga mea ki a koe, i mahi ai
koe ki reira: ko te hunga i hokohoko ki a koe mai i tou
taitamarikitanga, ka kotiti atu ratou ki tona wahi, ki tona wahi; kahore
he kaiwhakaora mou.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> ¶ Whakarongo ki tenei, e te whare o
Hakopa, e te hunga kua huaina nei ko Iharaira hei ingoa mo koutou, kua
puta ake nei i roto i nga wai o Hura; e whakaoati ana i te ingo o Ihowa,
e whakahua ana i te Atua o Iharaira, ehara ia i te mea i runga i te
pono, i te tika.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Ki ta ratou karanga hoki, no te pa tapu
ratou, e okioki ana hoki ki te Atua o Iharaira; ko Ihowa o nga mano tona
ingoa.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> He mea whakaatu naku nonamata nga mea o
mua; ae ra, i puta ano hoki aua mea i toku mangai, he mea korero naku;
kitea rawatia ake kua mahia e ahau, kua puta.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> I mohio hoki ahau he pakeke koe, he uaua
rino hoki tou kaki, he parahi tou rae;

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> Na reira naku i whakaatu ki a koe
inamata; kiano i puta kua korerotia e ahau ki a koe: kei ki koe, Na taku
whakapakoko ena mahi, he mea whakahau enei na te mea i whaowhaoa e ahau,
na te mea i whakarewaina e ahau.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Kua rongo koe; tirohia tenei katoa: a e
kore ianei e whakaaturia e koutou? Kua korerotia nei e ahau ki a koe he
mea hou, he mea i muri i tenei wa, he mea huna, kihai i mohiotia e koe;

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> He mea hanga nonaianei, kahore hoki
inamata: i mua i tenei ra kihai i rangona e koutou; kei ki koe, Nana, i
mohiotia e ahau.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> Ae ra, kihai koe i rongo, kihai i mohio;
ae ra, mai o mua kihai tou taringa i whakapuaretia: i mohio hoki ahau i
mahi tinihanga koe, a no te kopu ano koe i huaina ai he poka ke.

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> ¶ Ka whakaaro ahau ki toku ingoa, a ka
puhoi toku riri; ka whakaaro ki te whakamoemiti ki ahau, a ka pehi i
taku ki a koe, kei hatepea atu koe.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> Kua oti ou para te tahi e ahau, ehara
ia i te mea hei hiriwa; he mea whiriwhiri koe naku i roto i te oumu, i
te tangi.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> He whakaaro ki ahau, he whakaaro ki
ahau, i meatia ai tenei e ahau: kia whakapokea koia toku ingoa? e kore
ano toku kororia e hoatu e ahau ki tetahi atu.

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> Whakarongo ki ahau, e Hakopa, e
Iharaira, e taku i karanga ai; ko ahau ia, ko ahau te tuatahi, ko ahau
ano te mutunga.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> Ae ra, na toku ringa i whakatakoto nga
turanga o te whenua, na toku matau i hora nga rangi; ki te karangatia
ratou e ahau, ka tu ngatahi ratou.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> Huihui mai, e koutou katoa, whakarongo
hoki; na wai o ratou enei mea i whakaatu? He mea aroha ia na Ihowa; ka
oti i a ia tana i pai ai ki Papurona, ka pa ano tona ringa ki nga
Karari.

<span id="an_48:15">48:15</span> Naku, naku te kupu, ae ra, he mea
karanga ia naku, naku ia i kawe mai, ka tika ano i a ia tona ara.

<span id="an_48:16">48:16</span> ¶ Whakatata mai ki ahau, whakarongo ki
tenei; ko taku, no te timatanga ra ano ehara i te korero puku: i nga wa
o aua mea, i reira ahau; na, inaianei na te Ariki, na Ihowa ahau i unga
mai, na tona wairua ano.

<span id="an_48:17">48:17</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a tou
kaihoko, a te Mea Tapu o Iharaira, Ko Ihowa ahau, ko tou Atua e whakaako
nei i a koe ki te pai mou, e arahi nei i a koe i te ara e haere ai koe.

<span id="an_48:18">48:18</span> Aue, me i rongo koe ki aku whakahau,
ina, kua rite ki te awa te mau o te rongo ki a koe; ko tou tika, koia
ano kei nga ngaru o te moana.

<span id="an_48:19">48:19</span> Kua rite ano ou uri ki te onepu, nga
whanau o ou whekau ki te kirikiri o reira; ko tona ingoa kihai i hatepea
atu, kihai i whakangaromia i toku aroaro.

<span id="an_48:20">48:20</span> Haere atu i Papurona, e rere i roto i
nga Karari; kia waiata te reo i a koutou e whakaatu ana; korerotia
tenei, whakapuakina ki te pito o te whenua; ki atu, Kua oti i a Ihowa
tana pononga, a Hakopa te hoko.

<span id="an_48:21">48:21</span> Kihai ano ratou i matewai i a ia e
arahi ana i a ratou i nga koraha; i meinga e ia te wai mo ratou kia rere
i roto i te kamaka: i wahia e ia te kamaka, a pupu mai ana te wai.

<span id="an_48:22">48:22</span> Kahore he maunga rongo ki te hunga
kino, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> ¶ Whakarongo, e nga motu, ki ahau; kia
whai whakaaro, e nga iwi o tawhiti; na Ihowa ahau i karanga, no te kopu
mai ano; no nga whekau o toku whaea i whakahua ai ia i toku ingoa.

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> A meinga iho e ia toku mangai hei hoari
koi; huna ana ahau e ia ki te taumarumarunga iho o tona ringa; a meinga
ana ahau e ia hei pere kua oti te oro; kuhua ana ahau e ia ki tana papa
pere.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> I mea ano ia ki ahau, Ko koe taku
pononga; ko Iharaira, mau ka whai kororia ai ahau.

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> Ko ahau ia i mea, Maumau mauiui noa ahau,
he kore noa iho, he tekateka noa i whakapaua ai e ahau toku kaha; raia,
kei a Ihowa he whakawa moku, kei toku Atua hoki he wahi maku.

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> Na akuanei, e ai ta Ihowa, nana nei ahau
i whakaahua i te kopu hei tangata mana, hei whakahoki mai i a Hakopa ki
a ia, kia kohikohia ai a Iharaira ki a ia; ka nui hoki ahau ki te aroaro
o Ihowa, ko toku Atua hoki hei kaha moku;

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> Ae ra, i mea ia, He mea nohinohi kia
waiho koe hei tangata maku, hei whakaara i nga iwi o Hakopa, hei
whakahoki mai i nga oranga o Iharaira: ka hoatu ano koe e ahau hei
marama ki nga tauiwi, kia ai koe hei whakaoranga maku, a te pito ra ano
o te ao.

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, a te kaihoko
o Iharaira, a tona Mea Tapu hoki, ki ta te tangata e whakahawea nei, ki
ta te iwi e whakarihariha nei, ki te pononga a nga ariki, Ka kite nga
kingi, ka whakatika ano, ka koropiko hoki nga rangatira; he mea h oki na
Ihowa, he pono hoki ia, na te Mea Tapu o Iharaira; nana hoki koe i
whiriwhiri.

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa: No te ra
manakohanga atu i whakahoki kupu ai ahau ki a koe, no te ra whakaora
hoki i awhinatia ai koe e ahau; maku ano koe e tiaki, ka hoatu ano koe e
ahau hei kawenata mo te iwi, hei whakaara i te whenua, hei mea kia no
hoia nga kainga tupu kua ururuatia;

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> Hei mea ki nga herehere, Haere; ki te
hunga i te pouri, Whakaatu i a koutou: ka kai ratou ki nga ara, ka ai
hoki he wahi kai ma ratou ki nga pukepuke katoa.

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> E kore ratou e matekai, e kore ano e
matewai, e kore hoki te werawera, te ra ranei, e pakakinakina ki a
ratou; no te mea ko to ratou kaiatawhai hei arahi i a ratou; mana hoki
ratou e arahi ki nga puna wai.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> A ka waiho e ahau oku maunga katoa hei
ara, ka whakateiteitia hoki oku huanui.

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> Nana, ka haere mai enei i tawhiti;
nana, ko ena i te raki, i te taha hoki ki te uru, ko ena hoki i te
whenua o Hinimi.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> ¶ Waiata, e nga rangi; kia hari hoki, e
te whenua; kia pakaru mai ta koutou waiata, e nga maunga: ka whakamarie
hoki a Ihowa i tana iwi, ka aroha hoki ki ana kua tukinotia nei.

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Otiia i mea a Hiona, Kua whakarerea
ahau e Ihowa, kua wareware ahau i toku Ariki.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> Tera ranei e wareware i te wahine tana
kohungahunga, a kore ake ona aroha ki te tamaiti a tona kopu? E wareware
ano ratou: ko ahau nei, e kore ahau e wareware ki a koe.

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> Nana, kua taia koe e ahau ki nga kapu o
oku ringa; kei toku aroaro tonu ou taiepa.

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> Ka hohoro au tamariki; ka haere atu i
roto i a koe ou kaiwawahi, ou kaiwhakamoti.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> ¶ Tahuri ake ou kanohi a karapoi noa,
titiro hoki; ka huihui katoa ena, ka haere mai ki a koe. E ora ana ahau,
e ai ta Ihowa, ina, ka kakahu koe i a ratou, ano he mea whakapaipai, ka
herehere hoki i a ratou ki a koe, kei nga mea o te wahine marena hou te
rite.

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> Na, ko ou wahi ururua, ko ou wahi kua
tuheatia me tou whenua kua huna, he pono ka kopiri rawa koe mo nga
kainoho, a ka matara atu ou kaiwhakamoti.

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> Ko nga tamariki i whakapania ai koe,
tera ano ratou e mea ki ou taringa, E kiki ana te wahi nei moku:
whakawateatia atu, kia noho ai ahau.

<span id="an_49:21">49:21</span> A ka mea koe i tou ngakau, Na wai enei
i whanau ai ki ahau, kua whakakorea nei aku tamariki i ahau, he moke, he
parau, he kopikopiko nei ahau? na wai ra enei i whakatupu ake? Nana, i
waiho mokemoke ahau: ko enei, i hea ra enei?

<span id="an_49:22">49:22</span> Ko te kupu tenei a te Ariki, a Ihowa,
Nana, ka ara atu toku ringa ki nga tauiwi, ka tu hoki taku kara ki nga
iwi: a ka maua mai e ratou au tama, awhi rawa ki o ratou uma, ka kawea
mai hoki au tamahine i runga i o ratou pokohiwi.

<span id="an_49:23">49:23</span> A hei matua atawhai mou nga kingi, ko a
ratou kuini hoki hei kaiwhakangote mou: ka piko iho ratou ki a koe,
tapapa rawa ki te whenua, ka mitimiti hoki i te puehu o ou waewae: a ka
mohio koe ko Ihowa ahau; e kore hoki te hunga e tatari ana ki aha u e
whakama.

<span id="an_49:24">49:24</span> ¶ Tera ranei e tangohia nga taonga
parau i te tangata kaha, e mawhiti ranei te tangata kua tika nei tona
hereherenga?

<span id="an_49:25">49:25</span> Na ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Ina, ka
tangohia mai nga herehere a te tangata kaha, ka whakahokia mai ano nga
taonga parau a te nanakia: ka ngangare ano ahau ki te tangata e ngangare
ana ki a koe, ka whakaora hoki i au tamariki.

<span id="an_49:26">49:26</span> A ka whangaia atu e ahau to ratou
kikokiko ake ma ou kaiwhakatupu kino; ka haurangi ano ratou i o ratou
ake toto, me te mea na te waina reka; a ka mohio nga kikokiko katoa ko
ahau, ko Ihowa, e whakaora nei i a koe, ko tou kaihoko hoki, ko te Mea
Nui o Hakopa.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Kei hea ianei
te pukapuka whakarere o to koutou whaea, i whakarerea ai ia e ahau? Ko
wai ranei te tangata, i ahau ana moni, i hokona atu ai koutou e ahau ki
a ia? Nana, he kino no koutou i hokona atu ai koutou, na a kout ou mahi
whanoke ano i whakarerea ai to koutou whaea.

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> Na te aha i taku haerenga mai i kore ai
he tangata, he aha i taku karangatanga i kore ai tetahi e oho ake? kua
mutua koia toku ringa, te tau ai te araarai? kua kore ranei he kaha moku
hei whakaora? Nana, maku, ma taku kupu riri, ka maroke ai te m oana, ka
meinga ai nga awa hei koraha: piro ana o ratou ika i te waikore, ka mate
hoki i te matewai.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> E whakakakahu ana ahau i nga rangi ki te
mangu, uhia iho te taratara hei hipoki mo ratou.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> ¶ Kua homai ki ahau e te Ariki, e Ihowa,
he arero matau, kia mohio ai ahau ki te ata ngarahu atu i te korero ki
te tangata e mauiui ana. E whakaara ana ia i tenei ata, i tenei ata, e
whakaara ana i toku taringa ki te whakarongo kia pera me ta te hu nga
mohio.

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> Kua oti te whakatuwhera e te Ariki, e
Ihowa toku taringa, kihai hoki ahau i tutu, kihai i hoki whakamuri.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> Tukua atu ana e ahau toku tuara ki nga
kaiwhiu, oku paparinga ki nga kaihutihuti; ko toku kanohi kihai i huna
kei whakama, kei tuwhaina.

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> No te mea ka awhinatia mai ahau e te
Ariki, e Ihowa; koia ahau te whakama ai; koia i whakamarotia ai e ahau
toku kanohi ano he kiripaka; e mohio ana hoki ahau e kore ahau e
whakama.

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> E tata ana te kaiwhakatikatika moku; ko
wai hei whawhai ki ahau? kia tu ngatahi taua: ko wai he hoariri moku?
kia tata mai ia ki ahau.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> Nana, ko te Ariki, ko Ihowa, hei awhina
moku; ko wai hei whakahe i ahau? Nana, ka tawhitotia katoatia ratou ano
he kakahu, ka pau ratou i te purehurehu.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> ¶ Ko wai o koutou e wehi ana i a Ihowa,
e rongo ana ki te reo o tana pononga; ko te tangata e haere ana i te
pouri, kahore hoki he whakamarama, kia okioki ia ki te ingoa o Ihowa,
kia taupuhipuhi atu ki tona Atua.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> Nana, e koutou katoa e tahu na i te
ahi, e whitiki na i a koutou ki nga rama muramura; haere i te marama o
ta koutou ahi, i nga rama muramura hoki i whakangihaia na e koutou.
Tenei ta toku ringa mo koutou, ka takoto iho koutou me te tangi ano.

<span id="an_51:1">51:1</span> ¶ Whakarongo ki ahau, e koutou e whai na
i te tika, e rapu na i a Ihowa; titiro ki te kohatu i haua mai ai
koutou, ki te poka i te rua i keria mai ai koutou.

<span id="an_51:2">51:2</span> Titiro ki a Aperahama, ki to koutou
matua, ki a Hera hoki i whanau ai koutou: he kotahi hoki ia, karangatia
ana ia e ahau, manaakitia ana, whakanuia ana.

<span id="an_51:3">51:3</span> Ta te mea kua whakamarie a Ihowa i Hiona;
kua whakamarie ia i ona wahi katoa ka ururuatia, kua mea hoki i tona
wahi koraha kia rite ki Erene, i tona wahi titohea kia rite ki te kari a
Ihowa; he koa, he hari, ka kitea i roto, he whakawhetai, me te reo hoki
e waiata ana.

<span id="an_51:4">51:4</span> ¶ Whakarongo ki ahau, e aku tangata, kia
whai taringa ki ahau, e taku iwi: ka puta atu hoki he ture i roto i
ahau, ka takoto ano i ahau taku whakawa hei whakamarama mo nga iwi.

<span id="an_51:5">51:5</span> Kei te tata mai toku tika; kua puta taku
whakaora, ma oku ringa e whakawa mo nga iwi: ka tatari ki ahau nga motu,
ka okioki ki toku ringa.

<span id="an_51:6">51:6</span> Anga ake o koutou kanohi ki nga rangi,
tirohia iho te whenua i raro; ka memeha atu hoki nga rangi, ano he
paowa, ka tawhitotia te whenua, me he kakahu, ko te hunga hoki e noho
ana i reira ka apena te mate: ko taku whakaoranga ia ka mau tonu: e ko
re ano toku tika e heke.

<span id="an_51:7">51:7</span> Whakarongo ki ahau, e koutou e mohio na
ki te tika, e te hunga kei o koutou ngakau nei taku ture; kei wehi i te
tawai a te tangata, kei numinumi i a ratou taunu.

<span id="an_51:8">51:8</span> Ka kai hoki te purehurehu i a ratou, ano
he kakahu, ka pau ratou, ano he huruhuru hipi i te huhu: ka mau tonu ia
toku tika, taku whakaora ki nga whakapaparanga katoa.

<span id="an_51:9">51:9</span> ¶ Maranga, maranga, kakahuria te kaha, e
te ringa o Ihowa! maranga, kia rite ki nga ra o mua ra, ki nga
whakatupuranga onamata. Ehara oti i a koe nana i kotikoti a Rahapa, i
wero te tarakona?

<span id="an_51:10">51:10</span> Ehara oti i a koe nana i whakamaroke te
moana, nga wai o te rire nui? ko nga wai hohonu o te moana waiho ake e
koe hei huarahi haerenga mo te hunga kua oti te hoko.

<span id="an_51:11">51:11</span> Na, ko a Ihowa i hoko ai ka hoki mai,
ka haere mai ki Hiona, me te waiata ano ratou: i runga i o ratou mahunga
he hari e kore e mutu: ka whiwhi ratou ki te koa, ki te hari; a rere ana
te pouri me te aue.

<span id="an_51:12">51:12</span> Ko ahau, ina, maku koutou e whakamarie;
ko wai koe, e wehi na i te tangata e matemate nei, i te tama a te
tangata ka meinga nei hei tarutaru?

<span id="an_51:13">51:13</span> Ka wareware nei hoki ki a Ihowa, ki tou
kaihanga, nana nga rangi i hora, nana i whakatakoto te turanga mo te
whenua; ka pawera tonu koe i nga ra katoa i te riri o te kaiwhakawhiu, i
te mea e anga mai ana ia ki te whakamate? a kei hea te riri o t e
kaiwhakawhiu?

<span id="an_51:14">51:14</span> Hohoro tonu te wetekina o te herehere i
whakaraua; e kore hoki ia e mate, e heke ki te poka, e kore hoki e
whakakorea he taro mana.

<span id="an_51:15">51:15</span> Ko Ihowa ia ahau, ko tou Atua, i
whakakorikori nei i te moana, a hamama ana ona ngaru: ko Ihowa o nga
mano tona ingoa.

<span id="an_51:16">51:16</span> A kua hoatu e ahau aku kupu ki tou
mangai; kua hipokina koe ki te marumaru o toku ringa, kia whakatokia ai
nga rangi, kia takoto ai te turanga mo te whenua, hei mea hoki ki Hiona,
Ko koe taku iwi.

<span id="an_51:17">51:17</span> ¶ Maranga, maranga, whakatika, e
Hiruharama, i whakainumia nei e te ringa o Ihowa ki te kapu o tona riri:
kua inu koe i nga nganga o te kapu wiri, he mea tatau nau.

<span id="an_51:18">51:18</span> Kohore kau tetahi hei tautiti i a ia o
nga tama katoa i whanau i roto i a ia; kahore hoki tetahi o nga tama i
atawhaitia e ia hei pupuri i tona ringa.

<span id="an_51:19">51:19</span> Ka rua enei mea ka pono nei ki a koe;
ko wai hei tangi ki a koe/ ko te whakangaromanga, ko te wawahanga, ko te
matekai, ko te hoari: me pehea taku whakamarie i a koe?

<span id="an_51:20">51:20</span> Kua hemo au tama; e takoto ana i te
ahunga mai o nga ara katoa, ano he anaterope i roto i te kupenga; ki
tonu ratou i te riri o Ihowa, i te whakatupehupehu o tou Atua.

<span id="an_51:21">51:21</span> Mo reira, whakarongo ki tenei, e koe
kua tukinotia nei; e haurangi ana, raia, ehara i te haurangi waina.

<span id="an_51:22">51:22</span> Ko te kupu tenei a tou Ariki, a Ihowa,
ara a tou Atua, e tohe nei i ta tona iwi, Nana, ka tangohia e ahau te
kapu wiri i tou ringa, nga nganga o te kapu o toku riri; e kore e inumia
ano e koe a muri ake nei.

<span id="an_51:23">51:23</span> A ka hoatu e ahau ki te ringa o te
hunga e whakatupu kino nei i a koe, i mea ra ki tou wairua, Piko iho
nei, kia haere atu ai matou; na kua whakatakotoria e koe tou tuara hei
whenua, hei huarahi mo te hunga i haere atu ra.

<span id="an_52:1">52:1</span> ¶ Maranga, maranga; kakahuria tou kaha, e
Hiona; kakahuria ou kahu whakapaipai, e Hiruharama, e te pa tapu! no te
mea heoi ano haerenga mai ki a koe o te mea kokotikore, o te mea poke.

<span id="an_52:2">52:2</span> Ruperupea atu te puehu i a koe,
whakatika, noho iho, e Hiruharama: wetekina nga here i tou kaki, e te
tamahine herehere a Hiona.

<span id="an_52:3">52:3</span> Ko te kupu hoki tenei a Ihowa, Kua hokona
kautia atu koutou; na ehara i te moni mana koutou e whakahoki mai.

<span id="an_52:4">52:4</span> Ko te kupu hoki tenei a te Ariki, a
Ihowa, I haere atu taku iwi ki Ihipa i mua, ki reira noho ai; na kahore
he rawa i whakatupuria kinotia ai ratou e te Ahiriana.

<span id="an_52:5">52:5</span> Na he aha ra taku i konei, e ai ta Ihowa;
ka kahakina kautia atu nei hoki taku iwi? tangi aue ana i o ratou
rangatira, e ai ta Ihowa, e whakahaweatia tonutia ana toku ingoa i tenei
ra, i tenei ra.

<span id="an_52:6">52:6</span> Mo konei ka mohio taku iwi ki toku ingoa:
mo konei ka mohio ratou i taua ra ko ahau te korero nei; nana, ko ahau
tenei.

<span id="an_52:7">52:7</span> ¶ Ano te ahuareka o nga waewae i runga i
nga maunga o te kaikawe i te rongo pai, e kauwhau ana i te maunga rongo;
e kawe mai ana i te rongo whakahari o te pai, e kauwhau ana i te ora; e
mea ana ki a Hiona, E kingi ana tou Atua!

<span id="an_52:8">52:8</span> Te reo o au tutei! ka maranga i a ratou
te reo, ka waiata ngatahi; no te mea ka kite ratou he kanohi, he kanohi,
ua whakahoki a Ihowa i Hiona.

<span id="an_52:9">52:9</span> Hamama, waiata ngatahi, e nga wahi o
Hiruharama kua ururuatia; kua whakamarie hoki a Ihowa i tana iwi, kua
hoko i Hiruharama.

<span id="an_52:10">52:10</span> Kua huhua te ringa tapu o Ihowa ki te
aroaro o nga tauiwi katoa, a ka kite nga pito katoa o te ao i te
whakaora a to tatou Atua.

<span id="an_52:11">52:11</span> Maunu, maunu, haere atu i reira: kaua e
pa ki te mea poke; haere atu i roto i a ia; kia ma, e nga kai mau o nga
oko a Ihowa.

<span id="an_52:12">52:12</span> E kore hoki koutou e haere kaika, e
kore hoki e haere pera i te whati; no te mea ka haere a Ihowa i to
koutou aroaro; ko te Atua hoki o Iharaira hei hiku mo koutou.

<span id="an_52:13">52:13</span> ¶ Nana, ka mahi tupato taku pononga, ka
whakatiketiketia ia, ka hapainga ki runga, a ka tiketike rawa atu.

<span id="an_52:14">52:14</span> Pera i te tini i miharo ki a koe; i
kino iho hoki tona kanohi i to te tangata, tona ahua i to nga tama a te
tangata:

<span id="an_52:15">52:15</span> Waihoki he maha nga iwi ka tauhiuhia e
ia; a ka kopi te mangai o nga kingi ki a ia; no te mea ko nga mea kihai
i korerotia ki a ratou ka kitea, ko nga mea kihai i rangona ka mohiotia.

<span id="an_53:1">53:1</span> ¶ Ko wai i whakapono ki ta matou korero;
i whakaaturia ranei ki a wai te ringaringa o Ihowa?

<span id="an_53:2">53:2</span> Ka tupu ake hoki ia ki tona aroaro, ano
he rakau wana, me te pakiaka hoki i te oneone maroke, kahore ona
ahuareka, kahore hoki he pai; a ka titiro tatou ki a ia, te ai he
ataahua e minamina ai tatou ki a ia.

<span id="an_53:3">53:3</span> I whakahengia, i whakakahoretia ia e te
tangata; he tangata pouri, kua mohio hoki ki te tangi: a, i ahua huna
nga kanohi ki a ia; i whakakahoretia, kihai hoki tatou i whakaaro ki a
ia.

<span id="an_53:4">53:4</span> ¶ He pono, nana o tatou mate i pikau,
nana hoki i waha o tatou pouri: ko tatou ia i mea, i tukitukia, i patua
ia e te Atua, i whakawhiua.

<span id="an_53:5">53:5</span> Kahore, i werohia ia mo o tatou he, i
kurua mo o tatou kino: nona te whiunga i mau ai to tatou rongo, kei ona
karawarawa hoki he rongoa mo tatou.

<span id="an_53:6">53:6</span> Ko tatou katoa, ano he hipi, kua marara
ke, kua anga atu tatou ki tona ara, ki tona ara; na Ihowa ia i mea kia
tau iho ki a ia te kino o tatou katoa.

<span id="an_53:7">53:7</span> I tukinotia ia, i whakawhiua; heoi kihai
i kuihi tona mangai: ano he reme i arahina ia kia patua, me te hipi hoki
i te aroaro o ona kaikutikuti e wahangu ana, kihai i kuihi tona waha.

<span id="an_53:8">53:8</span> Na te tukino, na te whakawa, tangohia atu
ana ia; tena ko tona whakatupuranga, ko wai o ratou i whakaaro kua wehea
atu ia i te ao ora? he mahi he hoki na taku iwi i patua ai ia.

<span id="an_53:9">53:9</span> A ka whakaritea hei te hunga kino he
urupa mona; i te tangata taonga ia i tona matenga; ahakoa kahore ana
mahi tutu, kahore ano he tinihanga i tona mangai.

<span id="an_53:10">53:10</span> ¶ Otiia i pai hoki a Ihowa kia kurua
ia; nana ia i mea kia mamae. Ina meinga e koe tona wairua hei whakahere
mo te he, ka kite ia i tona uri, ka whakaroa i ona ra, a ko ta Ihowa i
pai ai ka ata oti i a ia.

<span id="an_53:11">53:11</span> Ka kite ia i ta tona wairua i uaua ai,
a tatu ana te ngakau: ma te mohio ki a ia ka whakatikaia ai te tini e
taku pononga tika; mana hoki o ratou kino e waha.

<span id="an_53:12">53:12</span> Mo reira ka hoatu e ahau he wahi mona i
roto i o te hunga nui, a ka tu ngatahi ia me te hunga kaha i te taonga:
mo tona wairua i ringihia e ia ki te mate, a i taua ngatahitia me nga
poka ke; nana hoki nga hara o te tini i waha, nana i wawao nga poka ke.

<span id="an_54:1">54:1</span> ¶ Waiata, e te pakoko, e koe kahore ano
nei i whanau: kia pakaru mai te waiata, hamama, e koe kahore ano kia
whakamamae: he tini hoki nga tamariki a te noho kau i nga tamariki a te
mea whai hoa, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_54:2">54:2</span> Kia rahi atu te turanga mo tou teneti;
kia maro hoki nga uhi o ou nohoanga: aua e kaiponuhia; kia roa ou taura,
kia u hoki ou poupou.

<span id="an_54:3">54:3</span> Ka tohatoha noa atu hoki koe ki matau, ki
maui; a ka riro nga tauiwi i ou uri; ma ratou ano ka nohoia ai nga pa
kua ururuatia.

<span id="an_54:4">54:4</span> Kaua e wehi; ta te mea e kore koe e
whakama; kaua ano e numinumi, ta te mea e kore koe e whakama; no te mea
ka wareware i a koe te whakama o tou tamahinetanga; a heoi ano
maharatanga ki te ingoa kino o tou pouarutanga.

<span id="an_54:5">54:5</span> Ko tou Kaihanga tau tahu; ko Ihowa o nga
mano tona ingoa; ko te Mea Tapu hoki o Iharaira tou kaiwhakaora; ko te
Atua o te whenua katoa ka huaina ki a ia.

<span id="an_54:6">54:6</span> ¶ No te mea kua karanga a Ihowa ki a koe,
ano he wahine kua whakarerea, kua pouri te ngakau, ano he hoa wahine o
te taitamarikitanga, i te mea kua mahue, e ai ta tou Atua.

<span id="an_54:7">54:7</span> He iti te wahi i mahue ai koe i ahau; he
nui ia nga atawhainga e kohikohi ai ahau i a koe.

<span id="an_54:8">54:8</span> He riri puhake, i huna ahau i toku kanohi
i a koe, he wahi iti; he aroha mau tonu ia toku e aroha ai ki a koe, e
ai ta Ihowa, ta tou kaiwhakaora.

<span id="an_54:9">54:9</span> He penei hoki tenei ki ahau me nga wai i
a Noa; i ahau i oati ra, e kore e hurihia ano te whenua e nga wai i a
Noa: waihoki ka oati nei ahau, e kore ahau e riri ki a koe, e kore ano e
whakatupehupehu ki a koe.

<span id="an_54:10">54:10</span> Ko nga maunga hoki ka riro ke, ko nga
pukepuke ka nekehia atu; tena ko toku aroha e kore e rere ke i a koe, e
kore ano e nekehia ketia te kawenata e mau ai taku rongo; e ai ta Ihowa
e atawhai nei i a koe.

<span id="an_54:11">54:11</span> ¶ E koe, kua whakawhiua nei, kua puhia
nei e te awha! kahore ano i whakamarietia, nana, maku ou kohatu e
whakatakoto, he pai hoki te kakano; ka hanga ano e ahau ou turanga ki te
hapira.

<span id="an_54:12">54:12</span> Ka hanga ano e ahau ou tihi ki te rupi,
ou tatau ki te karapanaka, ou rohe katoa ano ki nga kohatu whakapaipai.

<span id="an_54:13">54:13</span> A ka whakaakona e Ihowa au tamariki
katoa; ka nui hoki te rangimarie ki au tamariki.

<span id="an_54:14">54:14</span> Ka whakaturia koe ki runga ki te tika,
ka whakamataratia atu i a koe te tukino; e kore hoki koe e wehi; e kore
ano te pawera e tata ki a koe.

<span id="an_54:15">54:15</span> Nana, huihui noa ratou, ehara ia i te
mea naku: ko te tangata e huihui ana ki te whawhai ki a koe ka papahoro,
he mea mou.

<span id="an_54:16">54:16</span> Nana, naku i hanga te parakimete e
pupuhi nei i te ahi waro, e mau nei i te mea hei mahi mana; naku hoki te
kaihuna i hanga hei whakamoti.

<span id="an_54:17">54:17</span> E kore tetahi patu e hanga ana mou e
marohirohi: ko nga arero katoa e whakatika mai ana ki a koe ki te
whakawa, mau ano e whakahe. Ko ta nga pononga a Ihowa tenei, tuku iho,
tuku iho; naku hoki ratou i tika ai, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_55:1">55:1</span> ¶ E! e nga tangata katoa e matewai ana,
haere mai ki nga wai! me te tangata kahore ana moni; haere mai, hokona,
kainga! Haere mai, hokona he waina, he waiu; kaua he moni, kaua he utu.

<span id="an_55:2">55:2</span> He aha ra i hokona ai e koutou te moni mo
nga mea ehara i te taro, to koutou uaua mo nga mea e kore ai koutou e
makona? ata whakarongo mai ki ahau, a kainga te mea pai; kia ora hoki o
koutou wairua i nga mea momona.

<span id="an_55:3">55:3</span> Tahuri mai o koutou taringa, haere mai ki
ahau; whakarongo mai, a ka ora o koutou wairua, a maku e whakarite ki a
koutou he kawenata mau tonu, ara nga atawhainga pono i a Rawiri.

<span id="an_55:4">55:4</span> Nana, kua waiho ia e ahau hei kaiwhakaatu
ki nga iwi, hei rangatira, hei kaiwhakahau mo nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_55:5">55:5</span> Nana, ka karanga koe i te iwi kihai i
mohiotia e koe; ka rere mai ano ki a koe nga iwi kahore i mohio ki a
koe; mo Ihowa hoki, mo tou Atua, mo te Mea Tapu o Iharaira; nana hoki
koe i whakanui.

<span id="an_55:6">55:6</span> ¶ Rapua a Ihowa, kei kitea ana ia:
karangatia atu, kei tata ana mai ia.

<span id="an_55:7">55:7</span> Kia whakarere te tangata kino i tona ara,
te tangata mahi he i ona whakaaro; kia hoki ki a Ihowa, a ka aroha ia ki
a ia; ki to tatou Atua hoki, he nui rawa hoki tana mahi tohu.

<span id="an_55:8">55:8</span> Ehara hoki oku whakaaro i o koutou
whakaaro, o koutou hurarahi i oku huarahi, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_55:9">55:9</span> Ta te mea e ikeike ake ana te rangi i te
whenua, waihoki ko oku huarahi e ikeike ake ana i o koutou huarahi, ko
oku whakaaro i o koutou whakaaro.

<span id="an_55:10">55:10</span> Ka rite hoki ki te ua raua ko te
hukarere e rere iho ana i te rangi, a e kore e hoki ki reira; engari e
whakamakuku ana i te whenua, e mea ana kia whai hua, kia pihi ake, kia
homai ano he purapura ma te kaiwhakato, he taro ma te tangata e kai an
a:

<span id="an_55:11">55:11</span> Ka pena ano taku kupu e puta ana i toku
mangai: e kore e hoki kau, mai ki ahau; engari ka meatia taku i pai ai,
ka taea hoki taku i unga atu ai.

<span id="an_55:12">55:12</span> Ta te mea ka haere atu koutou me te
hari ano, ka arahina i runga i te rangimarie; ka pakaru mai te waiata a
nga maunga, a nga pukepuke, i to koutou aroaro, a ka papaki ringa nga
rakau katoa o te whenua.

<span id="an_55:13">55:13</span> He tataramoa i mua, ka puta ake he
kauri; he tumatakuru i mua, ka puta ake he ramarama: a ka waiho hei
ingoa ki a Ihowa, hei tohu mo a mua tonu atu, e kore e motuhia.

<span id="an_56:1">56:1</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Puritia te
whakawa, mahia te tika; no te mea ka tata he putanga mo taku whakaora,
he whakakitenga mo toku tika.

<span id="an_56:2">56:2</span> Ka hari te tangata nana tenei mahi, te
tama a te tangata e pupuri nei i a ia, mau tonu; e pupuri ana, a kahore
e whakapoke i te hapati, e tiaki ana i tona ringa kei mahi i tetahi he.

<span id="an_56:3">56:3</span> ¶ Kaua hoki te tama a te tangata ke, kua
hona nei ki a Ihowa, e korero, e mea, He pono ka wehea rawatia mai ahau
e Ihowa i roto i tana iwi; kaua ano te unaka e ki, Nana, he rakau maroke
ahau.

<span id="an_56:4">56:4</span> Ko ta Ihowa kupu hoki tenei mo nga unaka
e pupuri ana i aku hapati, e whiriwhiri ana i nga mea e paingia ana e
ahau, a e hopu ana i taku kawenata;

<span id="an_56:5">56:5</span> Ka hoatu e ahau he wahi ki a ratou i roto
i toku whare, i roto ano i oku taiepa, he ingoa ano e pai ake ana i o
nga tama, i o nga tamahine; he ingoa mau tonu taku e hoatu ai ki a
ratou, he mea e kore e hatepea atu.

<span id="an_56:6">56:6</span> Ko nga tamariki hoki a te tangata ke, kua
oti te hono ki a Ihowa, he mea kia mahi ai ratou ki a ia, kia aroha ki
te ingoa o Ihowa, kia waiho hei pononga mana; ko te hunga katoa e pupuri
ana, a kahore e whakapoke i te hapati, a e hopu ana i taku k awenata;

<span id="an_56:7">56:7</span> Ka kawea ratou e ahau ki toku maunga
tapu, ka whakahari ano ahau i a ratou i roto i toku whare inoi; ka
manakohia a ratou tahunga tinana, me a ratou patunga tapu i runga i taku
aata; no te mea ka kiia toku whare, He whare inoi mo nga iwi katoa.

<span id="an_56:8">56:8</span> He kupu tenei na te Ariki, na Ihowa, na
te kaikohikohi mai o te hunga o Iharaira i peia atu, Kua kohikohia era
ki a ia; ka kohikohi ano ahau i etahi atu ki a ia.

<span id="an_56:9">56:9</span> ¶ E nga kirehe katoa o te parae, haere
mai ki te kai, e nga kirehe katoa o te ngahere.

<span id="an_56:10">56:10</span> Ko ona tutei, he matapo katoa, kahore e
mohio; he kuri reokore katoa ratou, e kore e tau; he momoe, he takoto, e
matenui ana ki te moe.

<span id="an_56:11">56:11</span> Ae ra, he kuri apo kai ratou, kahore
rawa e makona; he hepara enei e kore e ngoto te matauranga; anga katoa
ana ratou ki tona ara, ki tona ara, ki te mea taonga mona i tona wahi, i
tona wahi.

<span id="an_56:12">56:12</span> Ko ta ratou ki, Haere mai, maku e tiki
he waina, kia nui ano ta tatou inu i te wai kaha; a ka rite te ra apopo
ki tenei ra, he ra kei runga noa atu tona nui.

<span id="an_57:1">57:1</span> ¶ Ka riro ki te kore te tangata tika, a
kahore e maharatia iho e te ngakau o tetahi tangata: e tangohia atu ano
hoki te hunga tohu tangata; te mahara tetahi, e tangohia atu ana te
tangata tika kei kite i te he.

<span id="an_57:2">57:2</span> Ka haere ia ki te rangimarie, ka okioki
ratou ki o ratou takotoranga, ka haere tena, tena, i runga i tona
whakaaro tapatahi.

<span id="an_57:3">57:3</span> ¶ Ko koutou ia, awhi mai ki konei, e nga
tama a te wahine makutu, e nga uri o te tangata puremu, o te wahine
kairau.

<span id="an_57:4">57:4</span> He takaro ta koutou ki a wai? ki a wai te
hamama nui o o koutou mangai, te whetero roa o te arero? He teka ianei
he whanau koutou na te poka ke, he uri no te teka,

<span id="an_57:5">57:5</span> Koutou, e tahu na i o koutou hiahia i
waenga i nga oki, i raro i nga rakau kouru nui katoa; e patu na i nga
tamariki i nga awaawa, i raro i nga pari kohatu?

<span id="an_57:6">57:6</span> Kei nga kohatu maeneene o te awa tou
whai; ko ena, ko ena te rota i a koe; ringihia ana e koe he ringihanga
ki ena, whakaekea atu ana he whakahere. E marie ranei ahau ki ena?

<span id="an_57:7">57:7</span> I runga i te maunga tiketike, aua noa atu
ki runga, i hanga e koe tou takotoranga, piki ai ki reira ki te mea
patunga tapu.

<span id="an_57:8">57:8</span> Kua oti ano tou whakamahara te whakatu e
koe ki tua i te tatau, i nga pou: kua hura hoki koe i a koe ki tetahi
atu, ehara i ahau, kua piki ki runga; kei te whakanui i tou takotoranga,
whakaritea ana e koe he kawenata ki a ratou; i matenuitia ano e koe to
ratou takotoranga i te wahi i kite ai koe.

<span id="an_57:9">57:9</span> I haere atu ano koe ki te kingi, mea rawa
ki te hinu, whakanuia ana e koe au hinu whakaranu; unga ana e koe au
karere ki tawhiti, whakaititia ana koe e koe ano ki raro rawa ki te
reinga.

<span id="an_57:10">57:10</span> Mauiui ana koe i te roa o tou ara;
otiia kahore koe i mea, Kahore he manakohanga, Kua kitea e koe e nui
haere ana tou kaha; koia koe te ruha ai.

<span id="an_57:11">57:11</span> I pawera koe, i wehi i a wai, i teka ai
koe, i kore ai e mahara ki ahau, i kore ai tou ngakau e mea mai? kihai
ianei ahau i whakarongo puku he wa roa i mua ra ano, na kahore ou wehi
ki ahau?

<span id="an_57:12">57:12</span> Maku e whakaatu tou tika; tena ko au
mahi, e kore koe e whai pai i ena.

<span id="an_57:13">57:13</span> ¶ Ka tangi koe, ma ou huihui koe e
whakaora; otiia ka kahakina ratou e te hau, ka riro katoa atu i te nga:
ko te tangata ia e whakawhirinaki ana ki ahau, mona te whenua, ka riro
hoki i a ia toku maunga tapu;

<span id="an_57:14">57:14</span> Ka ki ano ia, Opehia ake, opehia ake,
whakapaia te ara, hapainga atu te tutukitanga waewae i te ara o taku
iwi.

<span id="an_57:15">57:15</span> Ko te kupu hoki tenei a te Mea tiketike
o runga rawa, ko tona kainga nei kei nga wa onamata, ko tona ingoa ko
Tapu; ko te wahi e noho nei ahau kei te tiketike, kei te tapu, i te
tangata he maru rawa tona ngakau, he papaku, hei whakahauora i te w
airua o te hunga papaku, hei whakahauora i te ngakau o nga mea kua maru.

<span id="an_57:16">57:16</span> E kore hoki ahau e whawhai a ake ake, e
kore ano e mau tonu toku riri: pena ka pehia rawatia te wairua i toku
aroaro, me nga manawa i hanga e ahau.

<span id="an_57:17">57:17</span> ¶ He he no tona apo taonga i riri ai
ahau, i patu ai i a ia; i huna ahau i toku mata, i riri, a haere kotiti
ke ana ia i runga i te ara o tona ngakau.

<span id="an_57:18">57:18</span> Kua kite ahau i ona ara, ka rongoatia
ano ia e ahau: ka arahi ano ahau i a ia, ka whakahoki ano i nga
whakamarietanga ki a ia, ki ona tangata ano hoki e tangi ana.

<span id="an_57:19">57:19</span> Ko ahau te kaihanga o nga hua o nga
ngutu; Ka mau, ka mau te rongo ki te hunga i tawhiti, ki te hunga i
tata, e ai ta Ihowa; maku ano ia e rongoa.

<span id="an_57:20">57:20</span> Ko te hunga kino ia rite tonu ki te
moana ngarungaru; e kore e marino, heoi kei te aia ake e ona wai te
puehu, te paru.

<span id="an_57:21">57:21</span> Kahore he maunga rongo ki te hunga
kino, e ai ta toku Atua.

<span id="an_58:1">58:1</span> ¶ Kia rahi te karanga, kaua e kaiponuhia,
kia rite ki te tetere te nui o tou reo, whakaaturia ki taku iwi to ratou
poka ke, o ratou hara ki te whare o Hakopa.

<span id="an_58:2">58:2</span> He rapu ano ia ta ratou i ahau i tenei
ra, i tenei ra, e ahuareka ana hoki ki te mohio ki aku ara: me te mea he
iwi e mahi ana i te tika, a kihai i whakarere i te whakaritenga a tona
Atua, e ui ana ratou ki ahau ki nga whakaritenga o te tika, e a huareka
ana ki te awhi ki te Atua.

<span id="an_58:3">58:3</span> ¶ Ko ta ratou ki, he aha matou i nohopuku
ai, a kahore koe e titiro mai? he aha matou i whakapouri ai i o matou
wairua, te mohio mai koe? Nana, i te ra e nohopuku ai koutou e kitea ana
e koutou te ahuareka mo koutou ano; e akiakina ana hoki e kouto u a
koutou whakamauiui katoa.

<span id="an_58:4">58:4</span> Nana, ko ta koutou nohopuku, hei mea
totohe, hei mea ngangare, kia moto ai ki te ringa o te kino: kahore
koutou i nohopuku i tenei ra hei mea kia rangona ai to koutou reo i
runga.

<span id="an_58:5">58:5</span> Ko taku nohopuku ianei tenei i whiriwhiri
ai? he ra e whakapouri ai te tangata i tona wairua? He tuohu koia no te
mahunga o te tangata, ano he kakaho? he whariki i te kakahu taratara, i
te pungarehu, ki raro i a ia? E kiia ranei tenei e koe he no hopuku, he
ra e manakohia ana e Ihowa?

<span id="an_58:6">58:6</span> He teka ianei ko te nohopuku tenei i
whiriwhiria e ahau? kia whakatangorotia nga here a te kino, kia wetekina
nga paihere o te ioka, kia tukua te hunga e tukinotia ana kia haere noa
atu, kia wawahia e koutou nga ioka katoa?

<span id="an_58:7">58:7</span> He teka ianei ko te tuwha i tau taro ma
te tangata e mate ana i te kai, ko te mau mai ki tou whare i nga
rawakore i peia atu? kia hipokina hoki te tangata e tu tahanga ana, ina
kitea e koe; kia kaua hoki e huna i a koe i ou kikokiko ake?

<span id="an_58:8">58:8</span> ¶ Ko reira tou marama puta ai, ano ko te
puaotanga, ka hohoro ano ou mate te mahu; ka haere tou tika ki mua i a
koe, ko te kororia ano o Ihowa hei hiku mou.

<span id="an_58:9">58:9</span> Ko reira koe karanga ai, a ka whakahoki
kupu mai a Ihowa; ka tangi koe, a ka mea ia, Tenei ahau. Ki te
whakarerea atu e koe te ioka i waenganui i a koe, te kokirihanga atu o
te maihao, me te korero kino;

<span id="an_58:10">58:10</span> Ki te mea ano ka whai ngakau koe ki te
tangata matekai, a ka makona i a koe te wairua e pehia ana e te mamae;
ko reira tou marama puta ai i roto i te pouri, ka rite hoki tou pouri ki
te poutumaro:

<span id="an_58:11">58:11</span> Ka arahina tonutia ano koe e Ihowa, ka
makona ano tou wairua i a ia i nga wahi kore wai, ka whakakahangia ano
ou whenua; a ka rite koe ki te kari kua oti te whakamakuku ki te wai, ki
te puna hoki e pupu ake ana, e kore nei ona wai e poto.

<span id="an_58:12">58:12</span> Ka hanga ano e ou uri nga wahi kua
ururuatia noatia ake; ka ara ano i a koe nga turanga o nga
whakapaparanga maha; a ka huaina koe, Ko te kaihanga o te taiepa pakaru,
Ko te kaiwhakahou o nga wahi i nga ara hei nohoanga.

<span id="an_58:13">58:13</span> ¶ Ki te tahuri atu tou waewae i te
hapati, i te mea i tau i pai ai i taku ra tapu, a ka kiia e koe te
hapati he ahurareka, he tapu no Ihowa, he mea honore, a ka
whakahonoretia ia e koe, ka kore hoki e mahi i ou ara ake, e kite i au
ake e ahuareka ai, e korero i au korero ake:

<span id="an_58:14">58:14</span> Katahi koe ka whai oranga ngakau i roto
i a Ihowa; ka meinga ano e ahau nga wahi tiketike o te whenua hei hoiho
mou; ka whangaia hoki koe ki te wahi tupu a tou papa, a Hakopa: na te
mangai hoki o Ihowa te kupu.

<span id="an_59:1">59:1</span> ¶ Nana, kihai i mutua te ringa o Ihowa,
te tau ai te whakaora; kihai ano i taimaha tona taringa, te rongo ai ia.

<span id="an_59:2">59:2</span> Engari na o koutou he i wehe koutou ko to
koutou Atua, na o koutou hara ano i huna ai tona mata ki a koutou, te
whakarongo ai ia.

<span id="an_59:3">59:3</span> Kua poke hoki o koutou ringa i te toto, o
koutou maihao i te he; ko o koutou ngutu kua korero teka, ko o koutou
arero kei te whakapuaki i te whanoke.

<span id="an_59:4">59:4</span> Kahore he karanga ki te tika, kahore he
tohe ki te pono; ko te horihori to ratou okiokinga, e korero teka ana
ratou; ko to ratou hapu he nanakia, whanau ake te kino.

<span id="an_59:5">59:5</span> E paoa ana e ratou nga hua o te neke, e
hanga ana e ratou te whare pungawerewere: ko te tangata e kai ana i a
ratou hua ka mate, a ki te kopengia tetahi, ka puta he waipera.

<span id="an_59:6">59:6</span> E kore o ratou whare pungawerewere e tau
hei kakahu, e kore ano ratou e whai hipoki i a ratou mahi: ko a ratou
mahi he mahi na te kino, he mahi nanakia kei o ratou ringa.

<span id="an_59:7">59:7</span> E rere ana o ratou waewae i te kino,
hohoro tonu hoki ratou ki te whakaheke i te toto harakore: ko o ratou
whakaaro he whakaaro ki te kino, he whakamoti, he wawahi kei o ratou
ara.

<span id="an_59:8">59:8</span> Kahore o ratou matauranga ki te ara o te
rangimarie, kahore hoki he whakawa i o ratou ara; ko o ratou huarahi,
whakakopikopikoa ake e ratou: ko te hunga katoa e haere ana na reira, e
kore e mohio ki te rangimarie.

<span id="an_59:9">59:9</span> ¶ Na reira matara noa atu te whakawa i a
tatou, te mau tatou i te tika: e taria atu ana e tatou te marama, na ko
te pouri; te tiaho, na kei te haere nei tatou i te pouri.

<span id="an_59:10">59:10</span> E whawha ana tatou ki te taiepa ano he
matapo, ae ra, me te mea ko te hunga kahore he kanohi: e tutuki ana o
tatou waewae i te poutumarotanga me te mea i te ahiahi; he rite tatou ki
te tupapaku i roto i nga tangata pakari.

<span id="an_59:11">59:11</span> Kei te ngengere tatou katoa ano he pea;
ko to tatou rite kei te kukupa e tumutumu tonu ana. E tatari ana tatou
ki te whakawa, heoi kua kahore; ki te whakaora, otiia kei tawhiti atu i
a tatou.

<span id="an_59:12">59:12</span> Kua nui hoki o matou poka ke i tou
aroaro, e whakaatu ana hoki o matou hara i to matou he; kei a matou nei
hoki o matou poka ke, a ko o matou kino, e mohiotia ana era e matou;

<span id="an_59:13">59:13</span> He poka ke, he whakakahore ki a Ihowa,
he peka atu i te whai i to matou Atua, he whanoke nga korero, he
whakakeke; kua hapu, kua puaki i te ngakau he kupu teka.

<span id="an_59:14">59:14</span> Kua tahuri atu nei ki muri te whakawa,
ko te tika tu mai ana i tawhiti; kua hinga hoki te pono i te waharoa, a
kahore he tomokanga mo te tika.

<span id="an_59:15">59:15</span> Ae ra, kua kore te pono; a ko te
tangata e whakarere ana i te kino ka waiho hei taonga parau. Na ka kite
a Ihowa, ka kino ki tana titiro, no te mea kahore he whakawa.

<span id="an_59:16">59:16</span> ¶ Na titiro rawa mai ia, kahore he
tangata, miharo ana ia no te mea kahore he kaiwawao; na, kei tona ringa
he whakaora mona; ko tona tika, na tera ia i tautoko ake.

<span id="an_59:17">59:17</span> I kakahuria hoki e ia te tika hei
pukupuku, ko te whakaora hei potae ki tona mahunga; kakahuria ana e ia
nga kakahu o te rapu utu hei kakahu, ropia mai ana te hae hei koroka.

<span id="an_59:18">59:18</span> Ko tana utu ka rite ki a ratou mahi, he
riri ki ona hoa whawhai, he utu ki ona hoariri; ki nga motu hoki ka
homai e ia he utu.

<span id="an_59:19">59:19</span> Na ka wehingia te ingoa o Ihowa i te
uru, tona kororia i te rawhiti. Ka haere mai hoki ia ano he awa e taheke
ana, e aia ana e te manawa o Ihowa.

<span id="an_59:20">59:20</span> A ka haere mai te kaihoko ki Hiona, ki
te hunga o Hakopa e tahuri atu ana i te poka ke, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_59:21">59:21</span> Ko ahau nei, ko taku kawenata tenei ki
a ratou, e ai ta Ihowa: Ko toku wairua i a koe na, me aku kupu i hoatu e
ahau ki tou mangai, e kore e neke atu i tou mangai, i te mangai o ou
uri, i te mangai ano o nga uri o ou uri, e ai ta Ihowa, aianei a ake
tonu atu.

<span id="an_60:1">60:1</span> ¶ E ara, kia marama; kua tae mai hoki tou
marama, kua whiti te kororia o Ihowa ki a koe.

<span id="an_60:2">60:2</span> Tera hoki e hipokina te whenua e te
pouri, nga iwi e te pouri kerekere; ka whiti ia a Ihowa ki a koe, ka
kitea hoki ki a koe tona kororia.

<span id="an_60:3">60:3</span> A ka haere mai nga tauiwi ki tou marama,
nga kingi ki ou hihi, ina whiti mai.

<span id="an_60:4">60:4</span> Kia ara ou kanohi i tetahi taha, i tetahi
taha, titiro atu hoki; kei te huihui ratou katoa, e haere mai ana ki a
koe; ka haere mai au tama i tawhiti, ka hikitia hoki au tamahine ki nga
ringa.

<span id="an_60:5">60:5</span> Ka kite koe i reira, ka whakamaramatia,
ka wehi ano tou ngakau, ka nui; no te mea ka tahuri ki a koe nga mea
maha o te moana, ka tae ano ki a koe nga taonga o nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_60:6">60:6</span> Ka kapi koe i te kamera, he tini, i nga
kamera tere o Miriana, o Epa; ka haere mai era katoa i Hepa: me te mau
mai ano i te koura, i te whakakakara; ka kauwhautia ano e ratou nga
whakamoemiti ki a Ihowa.

<span id="an_60:7">60:7</span> Ka huihuia nga hipi katoa o Kerara ki a
koe, hei kaimahi mau nga hipi toa o Nepaiota; ka manakohia ratou ina eke
ki runga ki taku aata, a ka whakakororiatia e ahau te whare o toku
kororia.

<span id="an_60:8">60:8</span> Ko wai enei e rere nei ano he kapua, me
he kukupa nei, ki o ratou matapihi?

<span id="an_60:9">60:9</span> ¶ He pono ka tatari nga motu ki ahau, me
nga kaipuke o Tarahihi i te tuatahi, ki te kawe mai i au tama i tawhiti:
i a ratou, i ta ratou hiriwa, i ta ratou koura hoki, hei mea ki te ingoa
o Ihowa, o tou Atua, ki te Mea Tapu o Iharaira, no te mea ka oti koe te
whakakororia e ia.

<span id="an_60:10">60:10</span> Ka hanga ano ou taiepa e nga tangata
ke, ko o ratou kingi ano hei kaimahi mau: he riri hoki noku i patu ai
ahau i a koe, he manako ia naku i atawhai ai ahau i a koe.

<span id="an_60:11">60:11</span> Ka tuwhera tonu ano ou kuwaha: e kore e
tutakina i te ao, i te po, kia kawea mai ai nga taonga o nga tauiwi ki a
koe, kia arahina mai ai hoki o ratou kingi me ratou.

<span id="an_60:12">60:12</span> Ko te iwi hoki, me te kingitanga, e
kore e mahi ki a koe, ka ngaro; ina, ka moti rawa aua iwi.

<span id="an_60:13">60:13</span> Ka tae mai te kororia o Repanona ki a
koe, te kauri, te rimu, me te ake ngatahi hei whakapaipai, mo te wahi i
toku kainga tapu, a ka whakakororiatia e ahau te wahi o oku waewae.

<span id="an_60:14">60:14</span> Ka haere mai ano, ka piko ki a koe nga
tama a ou kaitukino, a ko te hunga katoa i whakahawea ki a koe, ka piko
ki nga kapu o ou waewae; a ka kiia koe, Ko te pa o Ihowa, Ko te Hiona o
te Mea Tapu o Iharaira.

<span id="an_60:15">60:15</span> ¶ He mea whakarere nei koe i mua, he
mea i kinongia, kahore hoki tetahi kia haere i waenganui i a koe, na ka
meinga koe e ahau hei mea nui e mau tonu ana, he kaonga ngakau ki nga
whakatupuranga maha.

<span id="an_60:16">60:16</span> Ka ngotea ano e koe te waiu o nga
tauiwi, ka ngotea te u o nga kingi: a ka mohio koe ko ahau, ko Ihowa,
tou kaiwhakaora, tou kaihoko, te Mea Nui o Hakaopa.

<span id="an_60:17">60:17</span> Ko te parahi ka whakaputaia ketia e
ahau hei koura, ko te rino ka whakaputaia ketia hei hiriwa, ka puta ke
te rakau hei parahi, ka puta ke nga kohatu hei rino; ko ou kaitohutohu
ka meinga he rongo e mau ana, ko ou kaiakiaki he tika.

<span id="an_60:18">60:18</span> E kore e rangona i muri te mahi nanakia
ki tou whenua; te whakamoti te wawahi, ki ou rohe; engari ka kiia, ou
taiepa, ko te Whakaoranga, ou kuwaha ko te Whakamoemiti.

<span id="an_60:19">60:19</span> E kore te ra e waiho i muri hei
whakamarama mou i te awatea; na, ko te marama e tiaho nei, e kore tera e
whakamarama i a koe; ko Ihowa hoki hei whakamarama mou ake ake, ko tou
Atua hoki hei whakakororia i a koe.

<span id="an_60:20">60:20</span> Heoi ano hekenga o tou ra, e kore ano
tou marama e pewa; no te mea ko Ihowa hei whakamarama pumau mou, a ka
mutu nga ra o tou tangihanga.

<span id="an_60:21">60:21</span> Ko tou iwi hoki, tika katoa, ka pumau
tonu ki a ratou te whenua; he peka whakato naku, he mahi na oku ringa,
kia whai kororia ai ahau.

<span id="an_60:22">60:22</span> To te mea nohinohi putanga ake, he
mano, to te mea iti, he iwi kaha: maku, ma Ihowa, e whakahohoro i tona
wa e rite ai.

<span id="an_61:1">61:1</span> ¶ Kei runga i ahau te wairua o te Ariki,
o Ihowa; na Ihowa nei hoki ahau i whakawahi hei kauwhau i te rongo pai
ki te hunga mahaki; kua unga mai ahau e ia ki te takai i te hunga ngakau
maru, ki te kauwhau ki nga whakarau kia haere noa, ki nga hereh ere, kua
tuwhera te whareherehere;

<span id="an_61:2">61:2</span> Kia karangatia te tau manako mai o Ihowa,
te ra rapu utu o to tatou Atua; kia whakamarietia te hunga katoa e tangi
ana:

<span id="an_61:3">61:3</span> Kia whakatakotoria he tikanga mo te hunga
katoa o Hiona e tangi ana, kia whakaputaia ketia o ratou pungarehu hei
ataahua, te tangihanga hei hinu koa, te wairua pouri hei kakahu
whakamoemiti; a ka kiia ratou he rakau na te tika, he mea whakato na
Ihowa, kia whai kororia ai ia.

<span id="an_61:4">61:4</span> ¶ Ka hanga ano e ratou nga wahi kua
ururuatia noatia ake, ka ara i a ratou nga wahi kua kore rawa i mua, ka
whakahoutia e ratou nga pa kua ururuatia, nga mea kua kore i era
whakatupuranga noa atu.

<span id="an_61:5">61:5</span> A ka tu te tangata ke, ka whangai i a
koutou hipi, ko nga tama ano a te tangata ke hei kaiparau ma koutou, hei
kaitiaki waina ma koutou.

<span id="an_61:6">61:6</span> Ko koutou ia ka kiia ko nga tohunga a
Ihowa, ka kiia koutou ko nga minita a to tatou Atua: ko nga taonga o nga
tauiwi hei kai ma koutou, ko to ratou kororia hei whakamanamana ma
koutou.

<span id="an_61:7">61:7</span> Mo to koutou whakama e rua nga whakautu;
mo te numinumi kau ka koa ratou ki ta ratou wahi: ae ra, i to ratou
whenua ka haere rua mai nga mea ma ratou, ka mau tonu hoki to ratou koa.

<span id="an_61:8">61:8</span> E aroha ana hoki ahau, a Ihowa, ki te
whakawa, e kino ana ki te pahua, ki te whakahaere he; ka hoatu ano e
ahau i runga i te pono ta ratou i mahi ai, ka whakaritea he kawenata mau
tonu ki a ratou.

<span id="an_61:9">61:9</span> Ka matauria ano to ratou uri i roto i nga
tauiwi, o ratou whanau i roto i nga iwi: ko te hunga katoa e kite ana i
a ratou ka mohio ki a ratou he uri no ta Ihowa i manaaki ai.

<span id="an_61:10">61:10</span> ¶ Ka nui toku koa ki a Ihowa, ka
whakamanamana toku wairua ki toku Atua; kua whakakakahuria hoki ahau e
ia ki nga kakahu o te whakaoranga, ropia mai ana e ia te tika ki ahau
hei koroka; ka rite ki ta te tane marena hou e kopare nei i te
whakapaipa i ki a ia, ki ta te wahine marena hou whakapaipai i a ia ki
ana mea whakapaipai.

<span id="an_61:11">61:11</span> Ka rite hoki ki ta te whenua e mea nei
i tona tupu kia kokiri ake, ki ta te kari e mea nei i nga mea kua
whakatokia ki reira kia tupu, ka pena ano ta te Ariki, ta Ihowa, ka
meinga e ia te tika me te whakamoemiti kia tupu ki te aroaro o nga iwi k
atoa.

<span id="an_62:1">62:1</span> ¶ He whakaaro ki Hiona i kore ai ahau e
noho hu, he whakaaro, ki Hiruharama te ata noho ai ahau, kia puta ra ano
tona tika ano he tiahotanga, tona whakaoranga ano he rama e ka ana.

<span id="an_62:2">62:2</span> A ka kite nga tauiwi i tou tika, nga
kingi katoa i tou kororia; a he ingoa hou e whakahuatia ki a koe, he mea
whakahua na te mangai o Ihowa.

<span id="an_62:3">62:3</span> Hei karauna ataahua ano koe i te ringa o
Ihowa, hei potae kingi i te ringa o tou Atua.

<span id="an_62:4">62:4</span> E kore koe e kiia a muri ake nei, He mea
whakarere; heoi ano kianga o tou whenua, He ururua; engari ka huaina
koe, ko Hepetipa; tou whenua, ko Peura: no te mea ka ahuareka a Ihowa ki
a koe, a ka whai tahu tou whenua.

<span id="an_62:5">62:5</span> Kei te marenatanga hoki o te taitamariki
ki te wahine te rite o te marenatanga o au tamariki ki a koe; kei te koa
hoki o te tane marena hou ki te wahine marena hou te rite o te koa o tou
Atua ki a koe.

<span id="an_62:6">62:6</span> ¶ Kua oti he kaitiaki te whakarite e ahau
ki ou taiepa, e Hiruharama; e kore e kopia te mangai i te ao, i te po. E
nga kaiwhakahua o to Ihowa ingoa, kei ata noho,

<span id="an_62:7">62:7</span> Kaua hoki e whakamutua ta koutou ki a ia,
kia whakapumautia ra ano a Hiruharama e ia, kia meinga ra ano hei
whakamoemiti i runga i te whenua.

<span id="an_62:8">62:8</span> Kua oatitia e Ihowa tona ringa matau,
tona takakau kaha, E kore e hoatu e ahau tau witi a muri hei kai ma ou
hoariri; e kore ano nga tangata ke e inu i tau waina i mauiui ai koe.

<span id="an_62:9">62:9</span> Engari ko nga tangata nana i whawhaki, ma
ratou e kai, whakamoemiti tonu atu ki a Ihowa; a ko nga tangata nana i
kohikohi mai, ka inumia e ratou ki nga marae o toku wahi tapu.

<span id="an_62:10">62:10</span> ¶ Tika atu, tika atu ma nga kuwaha;
whakapaia te ara o te iwi; opehia ake, opehia ake te huanui; kohikohia
atu nga kamaka; whakaarahia he kara ki nga iwi.

<span id="an_62:11">62:11</span> Nana, kua korero a Ihowa ki te pito o
te whenua, Mea atu ki te tamahine a Hiona, Nana, ko tou whakaoranga te
haere mai nei! nana, kei a ia tona utu, kei tona aroaro ano tana mahi.

<span id="an_62:12">62:12</span> A ka huaina ratou, Ko te iwi tapu, Ko
ta Ihowa i hoko ai; ka huaina ano hoki koe, He mea i rapua, He pa kahore
i mahue.

<span id="an_63:1">63:1</span> ¶ Ko wai tenei e haere mai nei i Eroma,
he mea rongoa mai nga kakahu i Potora? tenei he kororia rawa nei ona
kakahu, e haere ana i runga i te nui o tona kaha? Ko ahau e korero atu
nei i runga i te tika, ko te mea kaha ki te whakaora.

<span id="an_63:2">63:2</span> He aha i whero ai ou kakahu? i rite ai ou
weweru ki o te kaitakahi i te takahanga waina?

<span id="an_63:3">63:3</span> Na toku kotahi te takahanga waina i
takahi, kahore hoki he tangata o te iwi hei hoa moku: takahia iho ratou
e ahau, he riri noku; takatakahia ana ratou e ahau ki raro, i ahau e
weriweri ana; pati ana o ratou toto ki oku weruweru, whakapokea iho e
ahau toku kakahu katoa.

<span id="an_63:4">63:4</span> Kei roto hoki i toku ngakau te ra o te
rapu utu; kua tae mai ano te tau o aku i hoko ai.

<span id="an_63:5">63:5</span> Na ka titiro atu ahau, a kahore he
kaiawhina, miharo ana ahau no te mea kahore he kaitautoko ake: na kua
meatia e toku takakau, he whakaoranga moku; ko toku weriweri, na tera
ahau i tautoko ake.

<span id="an_63:6">63:6</span> Na takahia ana e ahau nga iwi i ahau e
riri nei; i ahau ano e weriweri ana ka whakahaurangitia ratou e ahau, a
ringihia ana e ahau to ratou toto ki te whenua.

<span id="an_63:7">63:7</span> ¶ Ka whakahuatia e ahau nga mahi aroha a
Ihowa, nga whakamoemiti ki e Ihowa, ka rite ki nga mea i homai e Ihowa,
ki a tatou; ki te nui hoki o te pai ki te whare o Iharaira i homai nei e
ia ki a ratou; he mea i rite tonu ki ana mahi tohu tangata, ki te nui
ano o ana mahi aroha.

<span id="an_63:8">63:8</span> I mea hoki ia, He pono, ko taku iwi
ratou, he tamariki e kore e korero teka: na ko ia to ratou kaiwhakaora.

<span id="an_63:9">63:9</span> I o ratou pouritanga ngakau katoa i pouri
ano ia, a whakaorangia ake ratou e te anahera o tona aroaro; he aroha
nona, he mahi tohu tangata i hoko ai ia i a ratou, hikitia ana ratou,
whakahaereerea ana i nga ra katoa onamata.

<span id="an_63:10">63:10</span> Heoi whakakeke ana ratou, whakapouritia
iho e ratou tona wairua tapu. Na ka puta ke ia hei hoariri mo ratou; kei
te whawhai ano ia ki a ratou.

<span id="an_63:11">63:11</span> Katahi ia ka mahara ki nga ra o mua, ki
a Mohi, ki tana iwi, i mea ia, Kei hea ia nana ratou i kawe ake i te
moana me nga hepara o tana kahuri? kei hea te kaiwhakanoho o tona wairua
tapu ki waenganui i a ratou?

<span id="an_63:12">63:12</span> I arahi nei i a ratou, he meatanga na
te ringa matau o Mohi, na tona takakau kororia? i wahi nei i nga wai i
to ratou aroaro, hei mea i tetahi ingoa mona e mau tonu ana?

<span id="an_63:13">63:13</span> I arahi nei i a ratou i waenganui o te
moana, ano he hoiho i te koraha, te hinga ratou?

<span id="an_63:14">63:14</span> Kei te kararehe e haere ana ki raro ki
te awaawa te rite, pera tonu ta te wairua o Ihowa meatanga i a ratou kia
okioki: pera tonu tau arahanga i tau iwi, i whai ingoa kororia ai koe.

<span id="an_63:15">63:15</span> ¶ Titiro mai i runga i te rangi,
matakitaki mai i runga i te nohoanga o tou tapu, o tou kororia; kei hea
tou ngakau nui, me au mahi nunui? ko te ohoohonga o ou whekau, ko au
mahi tohu ka pehia iho ki ahau.

<span id="an_63:16">63:16</span> He pono ko koe to matou papa, kahore
nei hoki a Aperahama e mohio ki a matou, kahore ano hoki a Iharaira e
mahara ki a matou: ko koe, e Ihowa, to matou papa; ko to matou kaihoko,
nonamata mai tou ingoa.

<span id="an_63:17">63:17</span> He aha koe, e Ihowa, i mea ai i a matou
kia kotiti atu i au ara, whakapakeketia iho e koe o matou ngakau kia
kaua e wehi ki a koe? Hoki mai, kia mahara ki au pononga, ki nga hapu o
tou kainga pumau.

<span id="an_63:18">63:18</span> He iti nei te wa i mau ai taua kainga
ki te iwi o tou tapu: e takatakahia ana tou wahi tapu e o matou hoariri.

<span id="an_63:19">63:19</span> Kua meinga matou kia rite ki te hunga
kihai nei koe i kingi mo ratou; ki te hunga kihai nei i huaina ki tou
ingoa.

<span id="an_64:1">64:1</span> ¶ Aue me i haehae koe i nga rangi, me i
heke iho, me i rere a wai nga maunga i tou aroaro!

<span id="an_64:2">64:2</span> Kia rite ki te ngiha o te ahi tahu rara,
ki te ahi e koropupu ai nga wai; kia mohiotia ai tou ingoa e ou hoariri,
kia wiri ai nga iwi i tou aroaro!

<span id="an_64:3">64:3</span> I tau meatanga i nga mea wehi kihai nei i
whakaaroa e matou, i heke iho koe, rere a wai ana nga maunga i tou
aroaro.

<span id="an_64:4">64:4</span> Kahore hoki kia rangona noatia i mua,
kihai i mohiotia e te taringa, kihai hoki te kanohi i kite i te Atua, ko
koe anake, e mahi nei i nga mea mo te tangata e tatari ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_64:5">64:5</span> Ko tau, he whakatau ki te tangata e koa
ana, e mahi ana i te tika, ki te hunga e mahara ana ki a koe i au ara.
Nana, i riri na koe, he hara hoki no matou; kua roa noa atu matou ki aua
ara, a ka ora ranei matou?

<span id="an_64:6">64:6</span> ¶ Ko matou katoa hoki kua rite ki te
tangata poke, a ko o matou tika ki te kakahu kua paru: e memenge ana
matou katoa ano he rau rakau; kei te hau te rite o o matou kino e kahaki
nei i a matou.

<span id="an_64:7">64:7</span> Kahore hoki he tangata e karanga ana ki
tou ingoa, e whakaoho ana i a ia ki te hopu i a koe: kua huna nei hoki e
koe tou mata ki a matou, a kua huna matou e koe na o matou he.

<span id="an_64:8">64:8</span> Na inaianei, e Ihowa, ko koe to matou
papa; ko matou te paru, ko koe to matou kaipokepoke; he mahi hoki matou
katoa na tou ringa.

<span id="an_64:9">64:9</span> Kaua, e Ihowa, e whakanuia rawatia te
riri, kaua hoki e mahara tonu ki te kino. Nana, titiro mai ra, he iwi
matou katoa nau.

<span id="an_64:10">64:10</span> He koraha kau ou pa tapu, he koraha a
Hiona, kua ururuatia a Hiruharama.

<span id="an_64:11">64:11</span> Ko to matou whare tapu, ko to matou
whare ataahua, ko te wahi i whakamoemiti ai o matou matua ki a koe, kua
waiho hei kanga ma te ahi, moti iho a matou mea matenui katoa.

<span id="an_64:12">64:12</span> Ka whakamanawanui ranei koe, e Ihowa,
ki enei mea? ka whakarongo puku ranei koe? ka nui rawa ranei tau
whakatupukino i a matou?

<span id="an_65:1">65:1</span> ¶ E rapua ana ahau e te hunga kihai nei i
ui ki ahau; e kitea ana ahau e te hunga kihai nei i kimi i ahau: i mea
ahau, Tenei ahau, tenei ahau, ki te iwi kihai nei i karangatia toku
ingoa ki a ratou.

<span id="an_65:2">65:2</span> Tuwhera tonu oku ringa i te ra roa nei ki
te iwi tutu e haere nei i te ara kahore i pai, e whai ana i o ratou
whakaaro ake,

<span id="an_65:3">65:3</span> Ki te iwi he whakapataritari tonu nei ta
ratou ki ahau ki toku aroaro, he patu whakahere i roto i nga kari, he
tahu whakakakara ki runga ki nga aata pereki;

<span id="an_65:4">65:4</span> E noho nei i nga urupa, e moe ana i roto
i nga wahi ngaro; e kai ana i te kikokiko poaka, a he hupa no nga mea
whakarihariha kei roto i a ratou oko.

<span id="an_65:5">65:5</span> Ko ta ratou kupu, Tu atu, kaua e
whakatata ki ahau; he tapu rawa hoki ahau i a koe. He paowa enei ki toku
ihu, he ahi e ka ana, a pau noa te ra.

<span id="an_65:6">65:6</span> Nana, kua oti te tuhituhi ki toku aroaro;
e kore ahau e whakarongo puku; ae ra, ka utua e ahau, ka utua ki roto ki
o ratou uma,

<span id="an_65:7">65:7</span> Ara o koutou kino, hui atu ki nga kino o
o koutou matua, e ai ta Ihowa, i tahu whakakakara nei ki runga ki nga
maunga, i whakaiti nei i ahau i runga i nga pukepuke: mo reira ka matua
mehuatia atu e ahau ta ratou mahi ki to ratou uma.

<span id="an_65:8">65:8</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Ka rite ki te
waina hou e kitea ana i roto i te tautau, a ka kiia, Kaua e whakakorea,
he manaaki hoki kei roto; ka pera ano taku e mea ai, he whakaaro ki aku
pononga, kei kore ratou katoa.

<span id="an_65:9">65:9</span> Ka whakaputaina ake ano e ahau he uri i
roto i a Hakopa, i roto hoki i a Hura, he tangata mona nei aku maunga:
ka riro ano a reira i aku i whiriwhiri ai, ka noho aku pononga ki reira.
