<span id="an_65:10">65:10</span> A hei puninga hipi a Harono, hei
tapapatanga te raorao i Akoro mo nga kau a taku iwi i rapu nei i ahau.

<span id="an_65:11">65:11</span> ¶ Ko koutou ia kua whakarere i a Ihowa,
kua wareware ki toku maunga tapu, kua whakapaia e koutou he tepu ma
Kara, whakakiia ana e koutou he ringihanga ki a Meni;

<span id="an_65:12">65:12</span> Ka tukua atu koutou e ahau ma te hoari,
ka tuohu koutou katoa, ka tukitukia: no te mea i karanga ahau, a kihai
koutou i whakao mai, i korero ahau, a kihai koutou i whakarongo; heoi
mahia ana e koutou te kino ki taku tirohanga, whiriwhiria ana e koutou
te mea kihai i paingia e ahau.

<span id="an_65:13">65:13</span> Na ko te kupu tenei a te Ariki, a
Ihowa, Nana, ko aku pononga, ka kai ratou, ko koutou ia ka matekai:
nana, ko aku pononga, ka inu ratou, ko koutou ia ka matewai; nana, ko
aku pononga, ka koa ratou, ko koutou ia ka whakama:

<span id="an_65:14">65:14</span> Nana, ko aku pononga, ka waiata ratou
he koa no te ngakau, ko koutou ia ka tangi i te pouri o te ngakau, ka
aue i te maru o te wairua.

<span id="an_65:15">65:15</span> A ka waiho ano e koutou to koutou ingoa
hei kanga ma aku i whiriwhiri ai, a ka whakamatea koutou e te Ariki, e
Ihowa, ka huaina hoki e ia he ingoa ke ki ana pononga:

<span id="an_65:16">65:16</span> Kia waiho te tangata e manaaki ana i a
ia ano i te whenua, mana ia e manaaki i runga i te Atua o te pono; ko te
tangata hoki e oati ana i te whenua, ko te Atua o te pono hei oati mana;
no te mea ka warewaretia nga raru o mua, a no te mea kei te huna atu i
oku kanohi.

<span id="an_65:17">65:17</span> ¶ Tenei hoki ahau kei te hanga i nga
rangi hou, i te whenua hou; e kore ano o mua e maharatia, e kore ano e
puta ake ki te ngakau.

<span id="an_65:18">65:18</span> Engari kia koa koutou, kia
whakamanamana ki taku e hanga nei ake ake; no te mea tenei ahau te hanga
nei i Hiruharama hei whakamanamananga, i tona iwi ano hei koanga ngakau.

<span id="an_65:19">65:19</span> Ka whakamanamana ano ahau ki
Hiruharama, ka koa ki taku iwi: e kore ano e rangona i muri te reo e
tangi ana, te reo e aue ana i roto i a ia.

<span id="an_65:20">65:20</span> Kahore o reira kohungahunga he torutoru
nei ona ra ake ake, kahore he koroheke kihai i rite ona ra; no te mea
kotahi rau nga tau o te taitamariki i tona matenga; ko te tangata hara
ia, kotahi rau nei ona tau, he mea kanga.

<span id="an_65:21">65:21</span> Ka hanga whare ano ratou, nohoia iho,
ka whakatokia he mara waina, ka kainga ano nga hua.

<span id="an_65:22">65:22</span> E kore e hanga e ratou hei nohoanga iho
mo te tangata ke, e kore e whakatokia hei kai ma tetahi atu tangata: no
te mea ka rite nga ra o taku iwi ki nga ra o te rakau, a ka roa aku i
whiriwhiri ai e ahuareka ana ki te mahi a o ratou ringa.

<span id="an_65:23">65:23</span> E kore ratou e mauiui noa, e kore e
whanau hei mate; no te mea he uri ratou no a Ihowa i manaaki ai, ratou
tahi ano ko ta ratou whanau.

<span id="an_65:24">65:24</span> Kahore ano ratou kia karanga noa, kua
whakao atu ahau; i a ratou ano e korero ana, ka rongo ahau.

<span id="an_65:25">65:25</span> Ko te wuruhi, ko te reme, ka kai tahi
raua; ko te raiona, ka rite ki te kau, ka kai kakau witi; ko te nakahi,
ko te peuhu hei kai mana. E kore ratou e tukino, e whakamate, puta noa i
toku maunga tapu, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:1">66:1</span> ¶ Ko te kupu tenei a Ihowa, Ko te rangi
toku torona, ko te whenua toku turanga waewae: kei hea te whare ka hanga
nei e koutou moku? kei hea hoki te wahi hei okiokinga moku?

<span id="an_66:2">66:2</span> Ko enei mea katoa hoki he mea hanga na
toku ringa, a na kona enei mea katoa i oti ai, e ai ta Ihowa; ko tenei
ia taku e titiro ai, ko te tangata e iti ana, kua maru te wairua, a e
wiri ana ki taku kupu.

<span id="an_66:3">66:3</span> Ko te tangata e patu ana i te kau, me te
mea e tukituki ana i te tangata; te tangata he reme nei tana patunga
tapu, me te mea he kaki kuri e poutoa ana e ia; te tangata e whakaeke
ana i te whakahere, me te mea e whakaeke ana i te toto poaka; te t
angata e tahu ana i te whakakakara, me te mea e manaaki ana i te
whakapakoko. Ae ra, kua whiriwhiria e ratou o ratou ara, e ahuareka ana
hoki to ratou wairua ki a ratou mea whakarihariha.

<span id="an_66:4">66:4</span> Ka whiriwhiria ano e ahau o ratou
whakaaro horihori, a ka kawea a ratou i wehi ai ki runga ki a ratou; no
te mea i karanga ahau, a kihai tetahi i whakao mai, i korero ahau, a
kihai ratou i rongo; heoi mahia ana e ratou te kino i taku tirohanga, a
whiriwhiria ana e ratou te mea kihai i paingia e ahau.

<span id="an_66:5">66:5</span> ¶ Whakarongo ki te kupu a Ihowa, e te
hunga e wiri ana ki tana kupu; Ko o koutou tuakana i kino ra ki a
koutou, i pei ra i a koutou, he whakaaro ki toku ingoa, i mea, Kia
whakakororiatia a Ihowa, kia kite hoki matou i to koutou koa; na ka
whakama r atou.

<span id="an_66:6">66:6</span> He reo, he ngangau, kei te pa, he reo kei
te temepara, ko te reo o Ihowa e whakautu ana i ona hoariri.

<span id="an_66:7">66:7</span> Kiano ia i whakamamae, kua whanau; kiano
i pa ona mamae, kua whanau he tane.

<span id="an_66:8">66:8</span> Ko wai i rongo i te penei? ko wai i kite
i nga mea penei? E whakamamae ranei te whenua i te ra kotahi? e whanau
ranei te iwi i te meatanga kotahi? whakamamae kau hoki a Hiona, kua
whanau ana tama.

<span id="an_66:9">66:9</span> Tera ranei e meinga e ahau kia taka te
ara, a kia kaua e whanau? e ai ta Ihowa; ka meinga ranei e ahau kia
whanau, a kopia iho te kopu? e ai ta tou Atua.

<span id="an_66:10">66:10</span> Kia koa tahi me Hiruharama,
whakamanamana ki a ia, e te hunga katoa e aroha ana ki a ia; kia hari
tahi me ia, kia hari, e te hunga katoa e tangi ana ki a ia.

<span id="an_66:11">66:11</span> He mea hoki ka ngote koutou, a ka
makona i te u, ara i ana whakamarie, he mea hoki ka whakatete koutou, a
ka ora te ngakau i te nui o tona kororia.

<span id="an_66:12">66:12</span> Ko te kupu hoki tenei a Ihowa, Nana,
ano he awa te rangimarie ka horahia atu e ahau ki a ia; ano he waipuke
te kororia o nga tauiwi: ko reira koutou ngote ai; ka hikitia koutou ki
ona kaokao, ka poipoia ki ona turi.

<span id="an_66:13">66:13</span> Ka rite hoki ki te tangata e
whakamarietia ana e tona whaea, ka whakamarie ano ahau ki a koutou; ka
whai whakamarietanga ano koutou i roto i Huriharama.

<span id="an_66:14">66:14</span> Ka kite koutou i tenei, ka koa o koutou
ngakau; ko o koutou whenua, koia ano kei te otaota te tupu; a ka
mohiotia te ringa o Ihowa ki ana pononga, tona riri ki ona hoariri.

<span id="an_66:15">66:15</span> ¶ Nana, ka haere mai a Ihowa me te ahi,
ko ona hariata koia ano kei te tukauati; ki te tuku i tona riri i runga
i te weriweri, i tana whakatupehupehu i roto i nga mura ahi.

<span id="an_66:16">66:16</span> No te mea he ahi ta Ihowa, me tana
hoari ano, ina totohe ia ki nga kikokiko katoa, ka tokomaha ano nga
tupapaku a Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:17">66:17</span> Ko te hunga e whakatapu ana i a ratou,
e pure ana i a ratou i nga kari, e whai ana i tetahi i waenganui, ko te
hunga e kai ana i te kikokiko poaka, i te mea whakarihariha, i te kiore,
ka pau ngatahi ratou, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:18">66:18</span> E mohio ana hoki ahau ki a ratou mahi,
ki o ratou whakaaro. Tenei ake ka huihuia e ahau nga iwi katoa, nga reo,
a ka haere mai ratou, ka kite i toku kororia.

<span id="an_66:19">66:19</span> Ka meinga ano e ahau he tohu ki roto i
a ratou, ka unga ano e ahau o ratou morehu ki nga iwi, ki Tarahihi, ki
Puru, ki Ruru, ki te hunga kukume kopere, ki Tupara, ki Iawana, ki nga
motu i tawhiti kihai nei i rongo ki toku rongo, kihai ano i kite i toku
kororia; a ka whakaaturia e ratou toku kororia i roto i nga tauiwi.

<span id="an_66:20">66:20</span> Ka kawea mai ano e ratou o koutou teina
katoa i roto i nga iwi katoa hei whakahere ki a Ihowa, i runga i te
hoiho, i te hariata, i te amo, i te muera, i te kamera tere, ki toku
maunga tapu ki Hiruharama, e ai ta Ihowa; ka rite ki ta nga tama a I
haraira e kawe nei i te whakahere i roto i te oko ma ki te whare o
Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:21">66:21</span> Ka tango hoki ahau i etahi o ratou hei
tohunga, hei Riwaiti, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:22">66:22</span> Ka rite hoki ki te rangi hou, ki te
whenua hou, ka hanga nei e ahau, a ka pumau tonu ki toku aroaro, e ai ta
Ihowa, ka pera te pumau o to koutou uri, o to koutou ingoa.

<span id="an_66:23">66:23</span> A tenei ake ka haere mai nga kikokiko
katoa i tenei marama, i tenei marama, i tenei hapati, i tenei hapati, ki
te koropiko ki toku aroaro, e ai ta Ihowa.

<span id="an_66:24">66:24</span> A ka haere atu ratou, ka matakitaki ki
nga tinana o nga tangata i he nei ki ahau: e kore hoki to ratou kutukutu
e mate, e kore ano to ratou ahi e tineia, a hei mea whakarihariha ratou
ki nga kikokiko katoa.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
